# **609 – Guides**

“Oh, you’re here, Alim, Mika!”

Yes, we had come to him when he called us. And yes, he had, once again, interrupted our intimate time. It was already the fourth occurrence, so we were naturally getting used to it.

“So, what new information did you learn?”

“Hrm, as We mentioned during our message exchange, We learned the name of the last Guide. Before We come to that, We want to speak about the Guide who destroyed the evil god.”

“Hm~.”

I didn’t know whether this was a necessary prerequisite, or if it was a tactic to heighten our expectations by delaying the information, but the conversation clearly wouldn’t proceed without it, so I yielded.

“The one who destroyed the evil god was said to be a young man who’d been found in a forest, suffering from amnesia. Moreover, the clothing he wore was unknown in Anazumu.”

“I… I see.”

“Indeed. And while he was young, he was strangely skilled with the sword. After he was taken in, he was said to have grown stronger at an astounding pace.”

_Huh~. From how it sounds, this boy who defeated Bufura’s evil god was from Earth like us._

Being found in the woods was similar to what happened to me. As for his sword skills… maybe he’d been talented from the start, just like Shuu with martial arts. Even assuming his memory loss was genuine, it was possible he kept his sword skills[1](#easy-footnote-bottom-1-120020).

Those who knew the same method I demonstrated during the dungeon training could grow strong extremely fast. And even without dungeons, you could grow strong quickly by hunting magic beasts in the wild at a faster pace than the people of this world.

“Then the king of that time took notice of the young man and made him the Guide. At that point, he was already SS-Rank… on the cusp of SSS-Rank even.”

“Really…?”

“Still, he was no match for you, Alim, who climbed the highest peaks of SSS-Rank as a minor.”

For a moment, I thought that this boy was incredible, but on second thought I realized that my own case was a lot more abnormal. Still, at the time, people likely saw it that way.

“Thus, said Guide and his partner, a sword he’d found in a dungeon, used mainly sword skills and the magic he could command through the vajra to defeat the evil god. He then sealed it in the vajra.”

Well, nothing up to this point was that unusual. I was able to defeat Samaeyl before I maxed out my stats.

“Still, it was only sealed and hardly destroyed at this point, right?” King Rama continued. “So, listen to this: the Guide wasn’t from this world, but from another one!”

_Oh, I see. Well, I already assumed that. There’s a surprising number of people from Earth_[2](#easy-footnote-bottom-2-120020) _who’ve come to Anazumu… come to think of it, Sages are also summoned here._

“You know about the Sages, I assume? They are brought here from another world, but the boy who became a Guide apparently wasn’t one and had strayed into this world instead. And his original world was said to be one without magic. In that case, why not take the evil god with him there? Keeping the vajra with the sealed evil, the Guide succeeded in finding a way to return to his world.”

“D-Don’t tell me that was how he destroyed it?”

“Exactly, there should be no way for an evil god to exist in a world without the concept of magic and concentrations of magic power. Thus, it is assumed to be destroyed.”

_So, he’s saying…_

_…that evil god is currently on Earth? He took it with him to another world, so it’s consider “destroyed” in Anazumu…?_

_Huh… hang on. Please don’t do that, it’s like dumping your trash in someone else’s home._

“Hrm, is something wrong, Alim, Mika? You do look adorably grumpy right now.”

“No, it’s nothing…”

“Uhm, will this other world be alright?”

“There’s no magic there, right? Why wouldn’t it be fine?”

True, it occasionally felt like this world was missing something, though maybe it was difference in thinking. Still, hearing its real history kept surprising me.

“So, to the main topic. Giving you prior information about the Guide who defeated the evil god was necessary… As for why, the man Our great grandfather designated as the Guide… had also come from another world.”

_Honestly… just how many people were sent to Anazumu…? Well, Mika and I came here after we died and our souls were saved, which was a net positive._

_Still, what about all the others? Where they brought here as a joke like Mr. Mitsuo…? Not like anything about that was funny._

“As We mentioned before, that Guide was a strange one. He made people laugh by performing various tricks without magic. He likely did it to earn money and it drew the attention of Our great grandfather. By talking to the man, he learned that he was from another world, so he made him the Guide.”

“In that case, is the reason your ancestor made him the Guide that he believed him somehow historically important?”

“Yes, you understand. Indeed, the diary mentions that he had high expectations for him.”

_Like he was the progeny of the Guide before him? They probably didn’t expect that another transmigrator would show up._

“So, what happened to this man afterwards?” Mika asked.

I was curious about that, too.

“It says that since he was so driven to return to his home, he left to search for a means to go back. While Our great grandfather had already made him the Guide, he still felt sorry for the man, so he gave him the advice to either ask the king of Yggdrasil, the country of the holy tree, or go to the Mephilad Kingdom where a means to return was said to exist. Due to the poor relationship of Our country with Yggdrasil, he recommended Mehilad.”

“And then…?”

“The Guide apparently went to Mehilad. Afterwards, his trail was lost.”

_A man from another world who came to the Mephilad Kingdom in search of a way home… hang on? I’m getting a bad feeling… a really bad feeling. And he was an entertainer, which sounds very much like a certain someone out there…_

“U-Uhm, just to make sure, could you tell us this Guide’s name, Your Majesty?”

“Of course, he was apparently called Mitsuo Lovelong[3](#easy-footnote-bottom-3-120020). A rather strange name.”

Mika and I looked at each other.

_How should I put it… it’s just as I feared._

#### **Footnotes:**

1. That might be the boy from the story in chapter 261, who was the cause of the Jizou statue being built.

2. I don’t get why he assumes everyone’s from Earth. There could be countless worlds out there.

3. The name is written in Katakana here. It is both possible that Mephistophales’ last name, which has the literal meaning of “love long” and which I’ve localized as “Aichou” so far, is meant to be pronounced as the English “Lovelong” or this might just be his performer name. At this point, I won’t change it unless there is a future instance that necessitates it.

+++

# **610 – The Clown and the Guide**

“Sorry, that was a bit much,” I muttered.

“Hm? There is still more to talk about…”

“C-Could we continue this another time?”

“What, did you come here even though you’re busy today? This was Our fault; we shall leave it for now.”

“My apologies, we’ll be off…”

Mika and I left the city and used an item that took us home without relying on Kanata’s power. In any case, there was a lot to sort through.

“…I never though Mr. Mitsuo would be the Guide.”

“True, but it makes sense,” Mika replied while scratching her cheek in a way that also propped up her head.

_What does she mean by that?_

“Why do you think so?”

“Look, didn’t he absorb the Demon God into his own body? The evil gods we fought so far… take Samaeyl, for instance. She possessed Karuna, one of the people with the power to find the Hero. And didn’t Surtr possess Shuu, one of the Sages? So, it was strange that Mr. Mitsuo, who’s neither Hero nor Sage, could absorb an evil god this easily.”

“If you put it that way…”

Evil gods couldn’t possess people who weren’t Hero, Sage, or those of a predisposition related to them… If such a law existed, there would’ve been no way for the Demon God to be absorbed into Mr. Mitsuo so easily, no matter how often he stored her in Droprot. I saw the whole process, and at no point had there been any visible rejection. If he was the Guide, then the easy process made sense.

_Heh-heh, Mika is as smart as always._

“But does he himself remember that he’s the Guide?” I wondered. “This must’ve been more than 100 years ago.”

“Didn’t he tell us that he slept most of that time? If it was like Urashima Tarou for him, he still might remember it.”

“Huh, I wonder. We’ll have to ask him…”

_But we can only go there once it’s Saturday on Earth. And that’s the day we promised to watch Shuu’s prefectural tournament._

“When are we going to talk to him?”

“I think Monday should work. We only have classes before noon until all the club tournaments are over.”

“Oh, that’s right!”

_In that case, let’s go ask him next Monday._

There probably wouldn’t be that many people since it was a weekday, which should make it easier to talk to him. While we did exchange our contact information, we could only ask him directly while the circus was still in town.

“The bigger issue is the evil god on Earth…”

“Right, that’s the scariest part.”

“The people of this world seem to think it won’t be an issue since you can’t use magic over there… If only if was that simple.”

_But doesn’t that mean the evil god really is rendered powerless? Hang on…_

“Didn’t all these strange events occur around the Jizou statue? Like that ball of flames someone saw.”

“Oh, yes, they did.”

“And Lord Jizou was the one who brought us to this world. And from what Shuu told us, there was a reaction when Rir performed the Anazuman prayer.”

“So, what you’re trying to say is that it might be possible to invoke magic on Earth, Ayumu? In that case, this ball of flames might have been the beginner spell Fireball.”

“Exactly.”

Mika’s expression darkened. If the phenomena I just mentioned were related to Anazumu and magic, then it might already be hopeless. We’d have no idea when and where the evil god would resurrect.

The ones we’d seen so far had used attacks that befitted the word “god” in their names, like scattering particles that caused instant death on contact (while ignoring any obstacles) or creating a different dimension. If such an evil god appeared on Earth, with neither magic nor magic tools available, the number of casualties would be immense.

Our level of technological development wasn’t that bad, so if guns and bombs were effective, it could prevent the destruction of the planet. Though it might still wipe out Japan and various other Asian countries.

“In that case, we need to find that vajra ASAP.”

“But we have absolutely no clue where it is.”

“Maybe Mr. Mitsuo knows something.”

“Well, he might, or he might not. Let’s ask him when we have the chance.”

_Still, have we really been in such danger up to this point? Living in a house without knowing an old bomb is buried beneath it is bad enough already. In any case…_

“How did they even bring the vajra to Earth?” I wondered.

“Bwuh?”

“I mean, when we go from Anazumu to Earth or vice versa, we can’t take anything with us, right? The only exception was when Shuu and the others were summoned as Sages.”

“Hm, that’s true. But it feels like there should be other ways. With this world being how it is, there might be a feature we can add to the Jizou teleporter.”

True enough, extraordinary things were normal in this world. If she put it like this, I couldn’t refute her.

“Hm~… What should we do?”

“Nothing happened so far, so we probably don’t have to rush our search. First thing is to talk with Mr. Mitsuo, and then we ask King Rama about the investigation.”

“You’ve got a point… Also, we’ll have to tell King Rama at some point that we’re not from Anazumu.”

“My gut tells me that he’ll practically force you to become the Guide, the moment he learns that.”

“Yes…”

Mika’s intuition was usually spot-on, so… the chance of the king conscripting me as the Guide was high.

+++

# **611 – Back at the Circus**

It was Monday, and Mika and I had gone straight to the circus. We obviously brought the lifetime pass. It was a weekday, so there weren’t as many people as last time.

“We ended up coming here again so soon.”

“Not like we have a choice. This is the quickest way to meet with Mr. Mitsuo.”

“True.”

After standing in line for a while, we arrived at the booth where you showed your tickets. We presented the woman at the counter with our pass.

“Can we use this?”

“Huh… oh, of course! This is valid! Please come over here.”

We apparently were to leave the line and go somewhere else. We were led behind the counter, where the receptionist entrusted us to another troupe member.

“I assume you’re the special guests the troupe leader informed us about. We welcome you. Regrettably, he is currently on stage…”

“Oh, I see.”

“We came here today to speak with Mr. Mitsuo,” Mika explained.

“In that case, please visit him after the next show ends,” the troupe member replied politely. “I shall inform him that you’re here… Since you queued up in line, do you wish to watch the performance? From the VIP seats, that is.”

“Yes, we’d love to see it!”

“You can talk to him afterwards, then.”

“Yes.”

It sounded like this troupe member would arrange our meeting. That was good to hear, since we had lots of questions. There was usually a 30-to-40-minute break between shows, so I had no idea if this was long enough for our talk, but it should suffice for the most important questions.

During the pause between shows, as guests entered and left the tent, we were led to the VIP seats. We were then given the menu for drinks and snacks. For now, we ordered two melon sodas topped with ice cream.

“Back at the circus… should we have brought Sakura and Kanata, too?” Mika wondered.

“Well, the reason we came here was to confirm new information and I don’t want to drag them into this affair. Kanata would probably dive in head first and Sakura would follow him.”

“That’s true.”

Indeed, Kanata’s brain was better than any computer, so he was reliable, but he tended to overdo it. And then he’d freeze up.

_Hang on, when did I start to see him like some machine? He’s human and my younger brother._

“Oh, it’s starting! We’ve been here just a short time ago, but it still feels exciting, doesn’t it?”

“It does!”

We took the drinks that had been brought to us and watched the show, only pausing to order French fries from the menu. Well, the performances obviously were the same as last time.

---

“Hah, that was fun!”

“It sure was.”

Even if it were the same performances, seeing them was still exciting. This time we were a bit more used to the VIP treatment and might have ordered a bit too much. We hopefully didn’t come over as ill-mannered guests.

“Hey there, you two! I see you’re back! Are you going to the troupe leader’s office?”

It was the same troupe member who’d shown me to Mr. Mitsuo the other day.

“Yes, could you bring us there?”

“Of course, please follow me!”

We did as asked. Before long, following the same route as last time, we arrived in front of the same office.

“That’s it for me.”

“Thank you so much for bringing them here,” Mr. Mitsuo told the man and then turned to us. “It’s good to see the both of you. You didn’t bring your younger siblings and friends today?”

“Yes, it’s just us.”

“I see. It seems you have things to discuss. Did something happen?”

There shouldn’t have been anything for the man to feel guilty about, but he still seemed strangely nervous.

_Well, whatever, I better get the ball rolling._

“No, we wanted to talk about something curious regarding Anazumu.”

“Oh, really?”

“Uhm, we learned that you were made the Guide of the Bufura Kingdom, around 100 years ago, Mr. Mitsuo. There was a record left behind in that country.”

The clown seemed confused.

“Around a hundred years ago… was it? Did you personally confirm that?”

“Yes, we did.”

“Well… it pains me to say this, but I have no memories of the time before I was reborn to lead the demons…

“I see…”

_So, that’s all he remembers…? I mean, it was more than a hundred years ago, so I guess it makes sense._

“S-Still, I am positive there was something strange about my status screen!” he continued hurriedly, possibly noticing my dejection. “That was likely the reason my skills worked on you, even with your higher level and stats.”

“Thinking about it this way, it makes sense…”

Back then, I had already been quite powerful and thought it strange that his Forced Contract worked without any issues.

“That is all I know. My apologies, I don’t remember much.”

“No worries, that was more than a hundred years ago, so it makes sense! I’d like to ask something else, are you still good on time?”

Mr. Mitsuo looked at the clock and then nodded.

“In that case… uhm, do you know about a vajra named Indra?”

“A vajra…?”

“Indeed, it is apparently the weapon used by the Guide to seal the evil god…”

“Huh, I see. No, I’ve never heard of it.”

Mika and I looked at each other. It didn’t seem as if the man knew anything in particular.

“Thank you for your time, even though we suddenly showed up to ask strange questions.”

“It’s fine, I should be the one to apologize since I was of no help.”

“That was all we came here for today.”

“Alright, please visit as often as you want while we’re in this city.”

Mika and I left the troupe leader’s office while bowing our heads to the man. From outside, we could hear him stand up and take out something.

+++

# **612 – To Ayumu’s Place**

It was the day after we paid another visit to the circus. In other words, Tuesday.

Today, classes also ended after only four hours. Before I started dating Mika, I’d spend such days by fully immersing myself in video games, but I could no longer do that. Come to think of it, I barely played those recently. That said, I usually got scolded if I did nothing but play games.

Our school was strict when it came to studying, so people were on edge with the end of the term just a few weeks away. Well, it was mostly the teachers, and the higher-ranking ones at that.

“That’s it for today. See~ ya,” the listless voice of the teacher on day duty today echoed through the room.

We got up in unison and shouldered our satchels.

“See you tomorrow, then.”

“Woof, see you!”

“Right, later.”

“Bye, you two.”

Shuu and Rir had club activities now. With the prefectural tournament in four days, they were training extra hard. I had confidence in Shuu stealing the show and emerging the champion of the national tournament.

_Huh, “Shuu stealing the show”, that’s almost a pun_[1](#easy-footnote-bottom-1-120026)_._

“What will we do today once we’re home?” Mika asked.

“Hm, what to do…”

We’d hung out in each other’s rooms for ages now, so we started to run out of things to do. We mostly played games. Recently, not sure if it was because of our stats, Mika started getting quite good at them. She’d been better than me at beat ’em ups and first-person shooters from the start, but that now also included virtual board games.

“Then how about we play a racing game today and the loser has to strip?”

“We can’t do that, we’re not in Anazumu…”

“Oh, you’re right.”

Every now and then, Mika wanted us to play strip versions of various games. I already knew what signs to watch out for. We were currently on Earth, so we couldn’t just do that.

“Mrr.”

“Is something wrong?”

She had suddenly stopped in place.

“No, I just got a feeling.”

“Your intuition? What does it tell you this time?”

“That we should pay the Jizou statue a visit, seeing it’s been a while.”

We actually visited the statue once per week, but we just finished two weeks in Anazumu, so it really felt like it had been a while.

“Let’s go there, then.”

“Alright!”

Thus, we made a detour to the statue on our way back home. We stood in front of it and folded our hands in prayer, though we had no idea if this was the correct way.

“How many years have we been coming here already?” I wondered.

“Let’s see, I’ve been coming here since one year before your family moved in, so… 16 years?”

“That would make it 15 years for me.”

_Time flies so fast… and the statue still is squeaky clean, you’d never think it’s decades or even centuries old. It’s incredible… as if it was made with material from Anazumu. Well, it was what sent us over there, so I guess it’s not impossible._

“Mh, alright, let’s go home.”

“Yep.”

We were about to leave and looked back. That moment, a man wearing a black hood entered my field of view. I couldn’t see his face.

“Huh.”

“When did he…”

It looked like Mika had seen him too, meaning I wasn’t hallucinating.

“Eh… what’s with that guy…”

“No clue…”

Could it be that he came here to abduct us? Not that I was positive about that, but we’d been in situations when it almost happened, so I was extremely wary.

“Huh… what a coincidence.”

“…?”

The way he spoke in undertones made him appear even scarier.

“Time passed quickly. The two of you have grown up and become quite beautiful.”

“Wh-Wh-What are you saying?”

From how he spoke, the man seemed to know us.

_But from where…?_

“Ayumu, didn’t your younger brother tell you about me?”

“Oh…”

_Right, this guy must be the suspicious man with the black hood Kanata mentioned. The one who knows about us._

“Y-Yes, he told us.”

“I see, ha-ha-ha-ha!”

_What’s going on with him? He seems super excited… Also, he said my name earlier. Even assuming he has a connection to Anazumu, no one from there except for Mr. Mitsuo should know my name._

“So, what’s this about?”

“Oh, I just wanted to see your faces. No other reason.”

“I-I see…”

“In any case, that’s farewell for now. We’ll surely meet again,” the hooded man spoke and then vanished with a poof, as if he were a ghost.

“…We’ll end up meeting him again, huh?”

“Probably.”

“Just what is this about…”

“There is no one in Anazumu who knew us when we were little, right?”

“There shouldn’t be.”

It was scary not knowing what this man’s goal was.

_Ugh… is that why Kanata told us to be ready to fight?_

“By the way, Ayumu.”

“Hm?”

For some reason, Mika seemed bashfully happy.

_What’s brought that on?_

“Uhm, thank you for always trying to protect me.”

“Ah, sure.”

Now that she mentioned it, she was right. At this point, I was probably doing it unconsciously.

“Eh-heh-heh…”

And even though we were in public, she kissed me on my cheek.

#### **Footnotes:**

1. In the original, he notices that 翔が優勝 (“Shou is the champion”), which reads as “shou ga yushou”, sounds like a pun.

+++

# **613 – To Shuu’s Place (Shuu)**

“Good work! From what I can tell, you’ll be unmatched at the prefectural tournament, too!”

“You think so, Instructor?”

Training was over for the day. Things were going great since we won the regional tournament in both the team and individual competitions. Even the teachers complimented us when they passed by.

“Oh, that reminds me, Fún. Could I ask you something?”

“What is it?”

“Do you prefer meat or fish?”

“Definitely meat! Absolutely!” the girl who was originally a wolfkin replied excitedly.

“Meat, huh… Alright, then at the prefectural… no, make that the provincial tournament and beyond. I’ll treat whoever performs well, be that individual or group fights, to Yakiniku! And if anyone manages to win the individual competition at the national tournament, he can bring any club member of his choice. I’ll treat them, too.”

“Whoa~~!?”

“Seriously!? Seriously!?”

It might have been limited to just a few people, but Gorilla Sensei was still quite generous. Even if it was the all-you-can-eat variant for 2500 yen, if all five of us managed good results at the provincial tournament, that’d cost him 12’500 yen.

_Hang on, what was that other part…?_

“Gorilla Sensei, do you think I’ll win the national tournament?” I asked him.

“You will, if you want me to treat Fún, too!”

“…Yessir!”

_Nothin’ else to do, I’ll have to win the national tournament. Can I do it…? Guess I gotta work hard._

“Anyway, it’s getting dark, so take care on your way back home, you two,” Gorilla Sensei told us. “Still, I guess they’d need to bring a whole army platoon to take you down, Hino.”

“I ain’t _that_ strong. Still, thanks, Instructor!”

“Thank you very much!”

Rir and I left the school. Our surroundings were dim. It was a nice atmosphere for walking home together as a couple. Like something that should be experienced in one’s youth.

“Please don’t overdo it, will you, Shuu?”

“I won’t, but I’ll make sure you’ll get to eat as much meat as you want. Paid by Gorilla Sensei.”

“Woof, thank you!”

She was about to hug my arm… but then stopped herself. It looked like she couldn’t shake her conviction that she smelled bad. Thus, I forcibly pulled her close.

“Woof, the smell!”

“Mine?”

“No, your smell is fine, Shuu. I’m talking about me.”

“You’re a super pretty girl, so I don’t mind.”

“Woof~…!” She turned red.

I didn’t get why a little praise made her blush that much after all that adult stuff we did in Anazumu… though it was awfully cute.

“S-Sorry, I’m still a bit sweaty.”

“I don’t mind.”

She hugged my arm. At this point, I was already used to feeling her soft breasts on my arm… not. No matter how much time passed, that never seemed to happen.

“Huh!?”

She suddenly seemed to notice something and looked back.

“What’s wrong, Rir?”

“Just now, it felt like there was someone there.”

She was staring fixedly at a single point. Likely realizing he had been found out, a suspicious man wearing a black hood appeared.

“…I didn’t think you’d notice me.”

“Why are you-”

“What’s this about? Do you want somethin’?” I demanded, stepping forward and interrupting Rir.

Somehow, it seemed like the hooded man was smiling.

“Huh, you’re Shuu, aren’t you? I remember you.”

“…So?”

“You were already manly as a child, but now you resemble a battle-hardened warrior. You’ve grown tall.”

“What!?”

Rir and I exchanged a momentary glance. If my guess was correct, then this was the guy connected to Anazumu whom Kanata mentioned.

“…Who are you?”

“You want to know my identity? I won’t tell. Let me ask in exchange; is that girl from Anazumu?”

“…Woof.”

Rir gave a twitch. I positioned myself so she was slightly behind me and could flee if necessary.

“What, I’m not trying to eat you… I see, you’re probably from one of the tribes. It is rare for someone from Anazumu to come to Earth. You might even be the first. That hair color, your keen perception[1](#easy-footnote-bottom-1-120028), and your sharp senses… you’re a wolfkin, aren’t you?”

“…Wh-What if I am?”

“Hrm, sounds like I hit the mark. I was just guessing.”

_What the hell is it with this guy? Is he here to harm us or not? Ugh, this is frustrating._

“Just what the hell is it with you?

“Hrm, this isn’t the time for you to know. You might find out when we meet again… At any rate, Shuu…”

The hodded man was staring at me… or so it felt.

“Wh-What now…?”

“It feels like you went through terrible hardship. Was there a time when you experienced burning rage?”

“…What?”

“It’s fine if you don’t remember. Farewell, for now.”

The hooded man vanished in a way that should have been physically impossible.

“What the hell was that about?”

“…Who knows. More importantly, you don’t have to make sure I can escape. We’re in this together if something happens. Rather, I should be the one to act as bait to allow you a chance for escape…”

“Rir, it’s a man’s job to protect the woman dear to him.”

“Shuu…”

She, once more, blushed adorably.

#### **Footnotes:**

1. In the original, this is 気配への完治 (“complete restoration of/towards indication/hint”) which is most likely an error and meant to be 気配への感知 (“perception of/towards hints”). 完治 and 感知 are homophones.

+++

# **614 – What’s Going On?**

“That creep showed up yesterday outside of my home.”

“…I see, so it happened to you too, Shuu.”

Yesterday, we had met the man wearing a black hood whom Kanata hat told us about. And apparently, it wasn’t just Mika and me, as Shuu and Rir also ran into him in the early evening.

Right now, I was at school, giving my best friend this information.

“What did he say to you?” Shuu asked.

“Well, more or less that he knows us. And that we’ll most likely meet him again.”

“I see. It was the same for me as Kanata’s experience; the guy talked as if he knew me from when I was a kid. He also guessed from Rir’s appearance and characteristics that she’s a beastfolk.”

“…So, on top of knowing all of us except Rir, he saw through her being from Anazumu and not human, even without her animal ears and tail present.”

_Grml, I can’t remember anyone who’d fit those criteria. If even Kanata, who can even remember things from when he was in the womb, doesn’t recognize this man, then there’s no way for us to._

“Oh, there are Rir and Mika…”

“Woof, that’s right.”

It looked like they were talking about yesterday’s events.

“And then, and then Ayumu stood in front of the strange man, as if to protect me. He looked so dashing!”

“Woof, Shuu did the same! He also told me to flee if anything were to happen…”

It sounded like they had a back and forth, comparing how Shuu and I acted at the time.

“Well, that’s only natural.”

“Yes, completely natural.”

Trying to protect the ones dear to you was obvious. Well, it wasn’t like the man had shown any indications of attacking us.

“…Incidentally, I just had a thought about the man in the black hood.”

“Woof?”

“Maybe it’s Lord Jizou… wouldn’t that be possible?”

“Woof!”

_Why did that thought never cross my mind?_

“What Mika and Rir just said…”

“I heard. Sounds possible,” Shuu agreed. “That god… if you can call him that… he sent you and Mika to Anazumu. If he’s been watchin’ over us since we were kids, it’d make sense that he knows up.”

“You’re right, that’s it! I’ll contact Kanata!”

Homeroom hadn’t started yet, so it probably was no issue if I contacted him. I used the communications app to send him information about Mika’s theory and Shuu’s encounter. The reply came almost instantly.

⟦I also had that thought.⟧

⟦You did?⟧

True enough, it would have been stranger if the genius hadn’t thought of that before. It was another loss for me as his older brother. In any case, he had never brought it up during our discussions…

⟦Indeed. But that can’t be true.⟧

⟦It can’t?⟧

_So, it’s wrong? Mika’s theory seems pretty sound… I wonder what’s wrong about it._

⟦Meowhy do you think that?⟧

⟦Meowhy, you ask… Look, didn’t that man seem impressed that we’ve become so big?⟧

⟦Oh, meow that you say it.⟧

⟦…Could we drop that weird cat speak?⟧

⟦Sorry.⟧

I was just joking a little, but it was enough to flip his lid. Hmph. In any case, I wanted to know his reasoning.

⟦This year alone, we paid several visits to the Jizou statue, didn’t we? Even before he sent you and Mika-nee to Anazumu. If he could see us here and over there… why would he word it in that strange way.⟧

⟦Hrm, if you look at it this way.⟧

The fact my brother had noticed that was a testament to his smarts.

⟦And that means…?⟧

⟦Well, that’s as far as I got.⟧

⟦Gotcha… Sorry for suddenly texting you.⟧

⟦Meow, it’s fine.⟧

_We might look like girls, but we still have these back-and-forths typical for brothers. Though maybe that’s just us. Anyway, since that theory seems to be a bust, we’ll have to start over from scratch._

“What did Kanata say?”

“He said that even though we’ve been at the statue only recently, the man talked as if he saw us for the first time in forever, so it’s probably not Lord Jizou.”

“Hah, makes sense. And here I though Mika’s idea made sense.”

“It’s rare for her, with her almost psychic precognition, to be wrong. Anyway, they seem to be getting really into that topic, so maybe we should tell them.”

“R-Right.”

Shuu and I gave Mika and Rir the explanation that didn’t really explain all that much. The two of them went from excitement to dejection.

“…Well, on second thought, it makes sense that Kanata already had the same idea.”

“Woof. So, what’s really going on?”

“…Who knows?”

We had no idea. We couldn’t even begin to guess. Since the only one who somewhat fit those criteria was Lord Jizou…

“Sit down, homeroom is starting. Today, classes will also only go for four hours.”

It was time and the teacher had entered the classroom. We went to our usual places and were left with nothing but to wrack our brains. Well, Kanata would probably figure something out.

+++

# **615 – The Prefectural Judo Tournament – 1**

For the next four days, I kept pondering the identity of the man in the black hood in some corner of my mind, but I couldn’t come up with anything, so I gave up on it until we found a clue.

More importantly, today was Shuu’s prefectural tournament. The team part of it, to be exact. If they won that, the provincial tournament would be next, and after that one the national. Making it to the national tournament alone was an incredible achievement.

_But I have faith that Shuu can win it!_

“Woof, you’ve all come to cheer!”

“Oh, Rir!”

She was wearing a judo uniform, which looked pretty good on her. You could see her large breasts through the thin fabric. This surely made it hard for the other club members to look at her. Or maybe they were used to it at this point.

Still, the only one with the privilege to actually do whatever he wanted with her was Shuu, the ball of muscles also known as my best friend. People were probably jealous of him. Not me, though, I had Mika.

“When I talked to Gorilla Sensei, he told me you can watch from the close seats! I’ll show you the way.”

“Thank you!”

The four of us followed her to the seats reserved for the judo club and family members who came to root for the team. The atmosphere here was great.

“Gorilla Sensei! I brought the cheerleaders!”

“Oh, Joujou and Magarigi. And your younger siblings. You can sit here.”

We sat down in the place the instructor indicated.

“Seeing you again makes it clear why people started to call Hino the Harem King.”

“Eh-heh-heh, they do?”

“Yes, with Fun in the mix, he’s now surrounded by five beauties…”

“I-I’m a boy!” Kanata, the second manliest of our group after Shuu, protested.

This was just as usual. Come to think of it, two years from now, Kanata would be under Gorilla Sensei’s care, if only for the judo classes.

“What, you’re a boy?”

“Yes, I am Joujou Ayumu’s younger **brother**!”

“Huh… you sure are a strange pair of siblings.”

“Ah-ha-ha, people often say that.”

They really did, and it was clear why it happened.

Next, Gorilla sensei turned his attention to Sakura.

“Oh? I feel like I know you from somewhere…”

“Ah, you’ve probably seen my younger sister on TV.”

“Oh, right! That one about the blind girl and her genius childhood friend…! I’m glad that you regained your eyesight, really… _sob_… really glad…”

“Th-Thank you.”

_Huh, is Gorilla Sensei a fan of these kinds of TV shows? How unexpected._

“So, that mean’s Joujou’s younger brother is that child prodigy!? What a small world.”

“I’m pretty sure they showed his last name in captions at some point…”

“I don’t remember these details.”

_Sounds like he didn’t watch very attentively. Yep, that tracks._

“…That reminds me, the two of you are currently second year middle schoolers, right? Are you attending the middle school portion of our school?”

“Yes, we are,” Kanata replied.

“Since you are Joujou’s younger brother, I’m sure you’ll join the…”

“Ah, I’m sorry. I’m pretty busy, so I probably won’t have time to join a club.”

“I-I see.”

The burly teacher deflated. It looked rather comical.

“L-Leaving that aside, shouldn’t the other club members arrive by now? It won’t just be Hino’s friends, but other club members who come to cheer too, right? Though even if just you, Joujou and Magarigi, were to root for them, I’m positive it’d boost their morale like crazy.”

“Sure, I’ll cheer with all my might!” I replied.

“Same here!” Mika agreed.

_Though it is possible that, just like in the regional tournament, neither Shuu nor vice-captain Gouda have a chance to shine today. Well… I can’t imagine they’ll be this dominant during the prefectural tournament._

“Oh, they’re finally here.”

Gorilla Sensei turned his head. There, the members of our school’s judo club were entering. Shuu was in front, forming the vanguard with the other members who’d participate in the tournament.

“We’re all set Gorilla Sensei. We can go at any time.”

“Good, Hino. Your friends have come to cheer you on.”

“I can see that. Thanks everyone.”

“Of course, we promised!”

Shuu’s expression was uncharacteristically sharp, which made him look quite handsome. If I was a girl, I might have fallen for him. Rir actually was staring at his face intently. When he noticed he went to pat her head with a gentle smile.

“Gorilla Sensei, are they here to cheer for the club head?”

“Yes, I’m sure you’ve seen them before.”

The club members turned their attention on us. Then, their eyes shone.

“Woah~, seriously!? Seriously!?”

“It’s Ali and Mika! Whoo!”

“What, you’ve come to cheer us on!? Really!?”

That was how it went. Boys generally only acted like this when it came to Mika and me. Though recently, that started to extend to Rir as well, and, according to Kanata, it also happened to Sakura with the middle schoolers since she stopped wearing her glasses. We were like full-fledged idols at this point.

“Hm, oh!? Weren’t you two featured in that documentary!?”

“Now that you mention it, they did have the same last names as Ali and Mika! I never realized!”

“I’m, I’m so happy you can see again!”

Indeed, they definitely treated Sakura the same way.

“With such illustrious guests and Fún who’s here to cheer you on as always, I’m sure you won’t mess up, will you?”

“””We won’t!”””

Gorilla Sensei had skillfully managed to raise their morale.

+++

# **616 – The Prefectural Judo Tournament – 2**

As I was talking with Shuu, a single member of the judo club came to us.

“Club Head!”

“Oh, that’s our vanguard, Hoshino.”

“Really?”

He was the only first-year in Shuu’s team. But even though he was younger than me, he looked incredibly burly.

“L-Little Ali[1](#easy-footnote-bottom-1-120136)! I-It’s such an honor to speak with you!”

“No need to be so formal. I’m not anyone special.”

“N-No, you the star of our school!”

True enough, people tended to treat me like a princess or idol. Though hearing them talk like that still felt awkward.

“In any case, do your best during the team competition! I’ll be rooting for you!”

Using the skills I cultivated in Anazumu to captivate those who’d already been infatuated with me, I lightly took his hand with both of mine and gave him a smile. It was all to cheer him on.

“I-I-I-I’ll give it my all!” he proclaimed with a bright red face.

_I hope they take the championship._

“Oy… don’t go seducing my junior, you hear?” Shuu, who’d seen the whole scene, rebuked me.

I tapped my own head lightly before sticking out my tongue.

“Tee-hee.”

“…”

Shuu shot me a downright frigid look.

_I see, I might’ve overdone it a little…_

“He does know that I’m male, doesn’t he?”

“Who knows. Apparently, half of the first years think you’re a girl.”

“Why would they when I’m wearing a boy’s uniform?”

“It’s probably your face.”

During our back and forth, two other burly boys closed in on Shuu.

“Ah, Hino, I’m sure you won’t get a turn today either.”

“Same for the vice club head.”

Indeed, those were the remaining two members of the team. The second and the middle.

“They’re reliable, aren’t they?” I asked Shuu.

“They sure are!” he confirmed.

“Oh, Little Ali!”

“Wow…”

While they were from another class and I wasn’t acquainted with them, they obviously knew me. There apparently wasn’t anyone in our school’s middle and high schools and the university who didn’t know about Mika, Shuu, and Me… and Rir too, at this point. Kanata and Sakura, who’d been on TV went without saying. Everyone knew them, except those who were completely oblivious like Gorilla Sensei. It had already reached an insane scale.

“What are your names?”

“They are called Futayama and Nakagawa. They have no resistance to women at all, so they’ll crumble if you do anything.”

“Huh.”

That was good to know. In that case, I had to make sure they’d do their best.

“Uhm, Futayama and Nakagawa?”

“Wh-Wh-What is it, Little Ali.”

“We might not always have the time to cheer our childhood friend on, so please make sure to root for him, too!”

_Heh-heh, maybe that works with those two._

I squeezed myself between the two of them and quickly put my arms around their shoulders. Then I whispered with an intentionally alluring voice in each one’s ears.

“Futayama, Nakagawa, you can lead Shuu… no, everyone to victory. I know you can do it.”

I winked at them, took a step back and patted their backs. With that, I was done.

“I’ll… do my best.”

“Hino, is this how it feels when a god plays a trick on you?”

“But he’s a boy. And he’s even taller than you, Futayama.”

“I don’t want to hear that from you.”

Later, I learned that Futayama was 165 cm tall, which meant that I was taller with my 170. Men often said that the woman being taller gave them a strange feeling, but it wasn’t that unusual for girls to be over 175 cm.

“It’s about time for the participants to go on stage,” Gorilla Sensei announced. “I don’t mind you gushing over Joujou, but don’t overdo it.”

“”””Yessir!””””

The moment they heard that, they immediately turned serious. It was pretty cool and gave me a better understanding about how girls who liked to watch sports felt.

On another note, it looked like the others had been talking to Gorilla Sensei. Well, if Mika were to speak to the club members, they’d end up completely drained like wrung-out rags. In my case, the people who knew that I was male were able to somewhat keep their composure, but they were putty in her hands.

More importantly, the participants had started going on stage while I wasn’t looking. All the fierce combatants who made it past the regional tournament were now gathered in the center. Wow… some of them seemed to be close to two meters tall. How was that even possible? In any case, Shuu looked so dashing, he stood out quite a bit. It was a bit awkward to call my childhood friend handsome, but it was the truth.

Shortly later, the opening ceremony ended and those who didn’t participate in the first match returned to their seats.

“Alright… next will be the first fight…!”

“…Uhm, I was thinking of going solo for the first match, if possible.”

“…Can you do it? This is the prefectural tournament.”

It was Hoshino who had made that crazy request. He nodded firmly at the question, seemingly having made up his mind.

“Somehow, I feel like I’ll be able to do it today.”

“…Alright. Do your best.”

“Yes!”

Whoever could’ve predicted this outcome? No one imagined that Hoshino would go through with his declaration.

#### **Footnotes:**

1. In the original he calls him “Ayu-chan-san” and I don’t even know where I’d begin to try to localize that, so I went with his known nickname “(little) Ali” instead.

+++

# **617 – The Prefectural Judo Tournament – 3**

“Hah, that idiot really did it.”

The first-year Hoshino had annihilated the opposing team during the first fight from their vanguard to their captain all by himself.

The venue had grown awfully noisy.

“I-Incredible…”

“Yes, he’s the second one who managed to pull that off during the prefectural tournament.”

“Huh, Gorilla Sensei, who was the other?”

“Hino.”

Come to think of, I did remember Shuu doing something to that account. I competed in the fighting tournament in Anazumu when I was still weak, so I could tell how abnormal that was.

“Hoshino… he was always unpredictable.”

“Shuu, what does he mean by that? That sounds a bit like he has a temper[1](#easy-footnote-bottom-1-120338).”

“He ain’t like that… To put it bluntly, his vigor and power differs dependin’ on time and situation.”

“Huh.”

Without interrupting Shuu and Rir’s conversation, Gorilla Sensei continued.

“He apparently trained in Judo ever since he was in preschool, but his talents didn’t bloom. Even when he reached high school, he still had that complex of being weak. But now that changed.”

“Well, Gorilla Sensei pretty much figured out his strengths right away,” Shuu explained, “and once he made sure to praise him enough, he got this strong.”

Hearing how amazing their instructor’s leadership skills were, confirmed what a great teacher the man was.

“You’re incredible, Gorilla Sensei!”

“You think so? Isn’t it natural for a teacher to do his best?”

“Wow.”

This guy was probably the coolest teacher at our school. Even with that face of his.

As we were talking, Hoshino returned, sporting a huge grin.

“Did you see that, everyone?”

“Yep, you were awesome.”

“That was incredible, Hoshino! You did great!”

Indeed, if praise made him so strong, then more compliments were in order. I did learn how to handle people in Anazumu.

“N-Not at all… ha-ha…”

“You were! You’re really strong!”

“I-I-I’m not that great… Heh-heh, thanks a lot.”

He seemed rather happy as he went back to his place.

Shuu was glaring at me.

“You’ve gotten good at that, huh?”

“At this point, I feel like I could become Ginza’s top hostess.”

“Hostess, not host, huh…”

“Yup.”

---

_“And the team from the — high school takes the championship! We’re now giving the word to their captain, Hino Shuu-“_

In the end, the remaining two matches were finished without even the vice-captain of the team ever getting a turn. I did notice that others started to call our school the “Monster High School”.

_Shuu is a given, but why are some pointing at me? I don’t get it, I’m not a monster!_

_“Of course, though I haven’t had anything to do as part of my team so far, so there’s not much I can say. Still-“_

It was a pity that Shuu needed to do the interview even though he hadn’t fought at all. The three members who participated in fights and gave it their all – especially Futayama and Nakagawa – were grinning broadly.

_“We know your achievements in the individual fights. It makes one wonder why your school produces this many outstanding athletes.”_

_“This is undoubtedly thanks to our instructor, Gorilla Sen- ah, my mistake-“_

The instructor seemed embarrassed when Shuu accidentally used his nickname. Indeed, a gorilla looking awkward, though that was probably a harsh way to put it.

_“Finally, could you show your enthusiasm for the provincial tournament?”_

_“Well, I feel no different than I did at the start, seeing I still have to fight my first match in the team competition, but I shall give it my all!”_

_“Of course, thank you for your words! Next will be a few words from the competitor who drew the most attention; the first-year Hoshino from — high school-“_

After Shuu’s interview ended, he alone came to us.

“…Hah~.”

“What’s wrong?”

“It’s nothin’, I was just thinkin’… why do I have to give this interview when I haven’t done anythin’ so far?”

“Now, now.” I patted his back.

_Hm~, there’s not even a single drop of sweat. In the end, he’s the coolest only when he can give it his all._

“Sorry, after you came all the way here to watch.”

“Not at all, your team won, so that’s a good thing. You can show off tomorrow,” I told him.

“Right, I will.”

“Oh, I can’t wait!” Mika agreed.

Shuu and I gave each other a thumb’s up. Mika joined in and did the same.

“Hey, does that mean Hino’s wife is Fún, and Ali and Mika are his mistresses?”

“Guess so.”

I felt like I heard a strange comment, but it was probably my imagination. Yep, definitely my imagination.

“Huh, what are the three of you doing? I want in, too!” Rir joined our conversation sounding somewhat enthusiastic.

Indeed, it was as if she’d been part of our group since forever… Come to think of it, what happened to my younger brother and future sister-in-law? I turned my head where they should be sitting.

“…I-I’m so happy you can see again…”

“Th-Thank you for saying that…”

They were surrounded by lots of people who likely saw them on TV and seemed to have a hard time.

#### **Footnotes:**

1. In the original, she wonders if Hoshino has a lewd side. I couldn’t think of a way to translate that into English while preserving the other meaning

+++

# **618 – The Prefectural Tournament’s Individual Competition – 1**

The four of us and all members of the judo club had gathered at the same venue as yesterday.

“Today is the individual competition.”

We had come once more to cheer Shuu on. As was mentioned just now, it was the individual fights, so we’d get to finally see Shuu in action!

“Sorry for draggin’ you here two days in a row.”

“It’s fine, we’re friends, aren’t we?”

“Right.”

“Heh-heh-heh.”

For some reason, he laughed, looking extremely happy. On that note, we did prepare a surprise for today.

“That reminds me, did you bring lunch boxes today, everyone?”

“Rir made mine… but since it’s from her, it’s all deep-friend stuff…”

“I think mine is onigiri,” a club member replied.

“Same for me,” another added.

_I see, it’s just as Mika predicted. Rir making fried food for Shuu was also within expectations. That means we can treat everyone._

After making eye contact with Mika, I brought out a big food-box from a nearby bag.

“Say, why don’t we all eat together at noon?”

“””Huh…!?”””

“We prepared it, you see. Since Rir only makes friend food.”

“Mika and I made something different. And we’ve got lots of it!”

The club members blinked in surprise.

“Of course, it’s all Mika’s, Sakura’s, Rir’s, and my home cooking!” I continued. “We planned for it and got up early in the morning to make it!”

“Come to think of it, Rir did seem busy in the morning…” Shuu mused, “so that was why.”

The club members gulped.

“U-Uhm, can we really eat the food you got in that box at noon?”

“Of course! You can eat the onigiri you brought as the main dish with side dishes from this! That offer obviously includes Gorilla Sensei.”

“Are you sure? That’s awesome!”

For some reason, a fire seemed to burn deep in the eyes of the club members. This had been another tactic to get their motivation up.

_Heh-heh-heh._

“I… I’m so glad I practice judo.”

“Yes, who’d have thought we’d get to eat home cooked food from three world-class beauties and a younger sister… is this a dream? This must be a dream.”

_Hm? Why did they mention Sakura separately after “three world-class beauties”? Mika, Rir, and Sakura should be those three, no?_

“Kanata didn’t cook anythin’?” Shuu asked as I was pondering. “Normally, he’d be all fired up to do somethin’ like this.”

“He said, ‘food you offer to others should be made by girls, so I won’t be so tactless to join you’ and refrained from cooking anything.”

“But you did join the cookin’, didn’t you?”

“Yes, I’m confident in my skills! Ever since I went to Anazumu.”

“…Are you really fine with that?”

“Huh?”

“…Oh, whatever. Guess you _are_ an idol.”

I didn’t really get what he meant. What exactly was the issue? Was it a mistake to make it since I wasn’t a girl and didn’t fulfill Kanata’s conditions? But Shuu usually ate whatever I made with a huge smile on his face. Hm~?

“Yes, rousing the spirits with lunch boxes is all well and good, but it’s almost time,” Gorilla Sensei interjected.

“Oh, completely forgot,” Shuu replied. “I’ll get ready, then.”

“”Right! Do your best!”” Mika and I told him.

“”You can do it, Shuu,”” Kanata and Sakura agreed.

“Please do your best, Shuu!” Rir exclaimed.

“I will.”

Seeing they were in front of others, Rir exercised some self-restraint as she hugged him. After separating immediately, Shuu showed a smile as he disappeared behind the stage. Rir also showed a small smile as she sat down next to Mika.

“Woof, we’ll be able to see Shuu at his best. This is what we came for.”

“You’re not wrong. But we should also cheer the other team members on, right?”

“Obviously! But I’ll still cheer for him with all my heart.”

Shuu really was loved… That was why he and Rir always got glares when they hugged at school. People were obviously jealous.

“In any case, it feels a bit sudden that Shuu is in the very first fight.”

“Right, there’s a reason for that.”

Gorilla Sensei had joined our conversation.

“What do you mean?”

“It’s because he was unmatched at the regional competition. If this tournament had them, he’d undoubtedly been seeded. Well, it’s a remnant of that. They’re trying to shame him.”

“I-I see.”

That meant he really showed a peerless performance. He was someone who could wipe out a dangerous gang by himself, so if he went all out, he could probably dominate the whole tournament by himself.

“There he is. Eh-heh-heh, he looks so cool.”

As his name, high school, and academic year was announced, Shuu entered the ring. Followed by his opponent.

Well, in the end, Shuu was quite handsome. Looking at him here, he seemed very different.

“…It’s starting.”

The referee arrived at their side. The competitors clasped their hands close to their obis and bowed.

_“Begin!”_

---

**Author’s note:**

I made another research related mistake: The individual competition in intra scholastic judo tournaments does not consist of a knockout tournament but uses a point system (likely related to the number of wins). To my chagrin, I ended up carried away with the competitive aspect of the story.

As for past examples like glasses which allow blind people to see well enough for their daily lives, those are far removed from reality. You might consider Earth in my setting an alternate reality, even before the first reincarnation in another world happens (though it might be our Earth’s future).

My deepest apologies. From now on, I shall disregard such things rooted in reality.

+++

# **619 – The Prefectural Tournament’s Individual Competition – 2**

_“One full point!”_

“As I thought, it was over in an instant.”

“Hah… woof… hah, hah… woof…”

“”””What!?””””

I couldn’t help making a double-take. The ones who had blurted out at the same time in surprise were Mika, Kanata, Sakura, and me.

It wasn’t that I couldn’t see what had happened. Thanks to Secret Martial Technique, I had the skills of a professional fighter. But even from that perspective, Shuu was abnormal. Rather, he was practically monstrous.

It was only a scant few seconds since the match had started. Up to the point when the two fighters grabbed each other, things were normal. Afterwards, however, it was as if we had entered a different dimension and before I knew it, the referee, somewhat late, was calling out a full point.

“So, it’ll go the same way even at the prefectural tournament.”

“Hah… hah… _gulp_.”

I did make Shuu fight tons of robotic judoka (and sometimes even those from other martial disciplines) and this was the result.

“Our childhood friend is no longer human.”

“Right. I can no longer tell what’s going on.”

“In any case, Rir has been acting strange for some time.”

“Huh?”

When I looked her way, her cheeks were bright red in excitement, she was breathing rapidly with her mouth half open, and her gaze was fixed intently on Shuu. She seemed to be struggling to get air, with one hand clutching her chest and the other between her thighs. If I had to describe how she appeared in fewer words, I’d say she was in heat. I felt sorry for my best friend.

“Rir, are you alright?”

“Shuu’s so cool… hah~… way too cool… hah~… hah… Oh, I’m sorry, you two.”

It took quite some time until she seemed to notice and replied to us. Her expression was like nothing she’d ever shown us before.

“Why were you in that state?”

“A-As a wolfkin woman… a female of a warlike tribe, I, uhm, love it when two men fight like this.”

“Oh, I see.”

She took a deep breath. It looked like she had more to say.

“So, when my lover Shuu, with his slim physique yet high muscle density – the very incarnation of muscularity, who makes me swoon by just looking at him – does so well in this tournament… that is to say, crushes an opponent, who’s at least stronger than those he faced in the regional tournament, with an overwhelming difference in skill…! It’s way too cool… I just… can’t…”

“Whoa there, calm down, Rir.”

Mika was rubbing Rir’s back, as the latter more and more lost herself.

_I see, from her perspective, Shuu is the perfect man. The ideal among ideals._

I couldn’t imagine anyone expected her to act like this. Still, she did have an incredible vocabulary in Japanese. It had improved so fast.

“Is Fún fine?” Gorilla Sensei asked worriedly.

“…She should be.”

“Alright, she did act similarly after Hino won the previous tournament… though it was worse this time.”

“I see…”

“Indeed. Thankfully, the other team members are too caught up in the match to notice, but it would be quite an issue if anyone saw her like that.”

Yes, if anyone other than us or adults with good self-control like Gorilla Sensei saw her now, they might end up stimulated in various ways. The inclinations of members of warlike tribes seemed quite problematic.

While all this took place, her future husband made his way back to us.

“I won! Two more and I’m off to the provincial tournament!”

“Good work.”

“You did a great job!”

“Shuu… Shuu, you were amazing right now…”

“Y-You think so? Hang on, Rir, why’s your face all red? It stands out a lot since your skin’s usually so light…”

“Ah~…”

Mika silently moved from the seat next to Rir to the one opposite mine. Shuu then sat down between his girlfriend and me. The moment he did, she clamped down on his arm.

“Wh-What now? Somehow, you always act this strangely after my matches.”

“Don’t worry about it… Right now, we could do anything even in front of others. We could even sneak off and have a quickie. If you want to, you could tie me up and get rough…”

“W-We ain’t ever done stuff like that!?”

_Nope, I didn’t hear anything._

Luckily, it seemed like only Mika and I heard their words just now.

“Hah… In that case, you can look forward to tomorrow.”

“R-R-Right.”

It sounded like they’d get busy during our next week in Anazumu.

“Hey, Rir.”

“_Huff_, what is it, Shuu?”

“For now, calm down. This wasn’t my last fight.”

“…Woof!”

She hugged him even more strongly. When the other club members finally noticed what was happening, a ton of jealousy was directed at them. Mika suddenly hugged my arm, too.

“…I got jealous of Rir, so just let me have that, alright?”

“That’s fine for me…”

_It got even Mika and me jealous…_

With that thought, I looked around and found the others shower us with warm gazes. What was going on now?

+++

# **620 – The Prefectural Tournament’s Individual Competition – 3**

“For now, all the club members who advanced to the prefectural tournament in the individual fights have finished their first fight.”

It was the five members of the team participating in the team fight plus three other club members who’d made it this far. And each of them had won their first fight. It confirmed, once again, just how strong our school’s judo club was.

“It’s time for lunch!”

“”””Whoo~~~!””””

All of them seemed incredibly hyped up. Seeing them so excited for our cooking made me happy.

“We’ll show you what’s in there, then!”

I opened the food box I had brought with me. Mika and Rir also opened the boxes they had brought.

“””Whoa~~…!”””

Everyone’s eyes were shining at the dishes laid out in front of them. Rir’s box contained all manners of fried food, from shrimp over fish and squid up to mini croquettes. Mine consisted of simmered dishes like seasoned eggs, and lotus and konjac roots. Mika and Sakura had prepared refreshing vegetable-based dishes like potato salad, asparagus wrapped in bacon, and small sandwiches. And finally, each of us also brought karaage and rolled eggs.

What about the cost, you ask? For some reason, Kanata had brought out a ton of money, telling us “I figured something like this might happen, so I set aside several thousand yen for you to use as you like”. My heart almost jumped out of my throat when he just plopped it on the table.

I honestly didn’t like relying on my younger brother that much, but he kept telling us not to worry about it, so that was what we ultimately did. From what he said, he made this much money in no time at all.

_I can no longer tell in what kind of dimension I’m living._

All the people around me, including Shuu, were straight up monsters. At this point, Kanata had probably earned hundreds of millions of Yen.

“Hang on, everyone, calm down. Let’s first show our gratitude to the four people who first came here to cheer and now even prepared lunch for us.”

“”””Thank you very much!!””

As one would expect of a sports club, their coordination and volume when giving thanks was on a different level. They also bowed their heads deeply.

“…Alright, let’s eat!”

There was a bang as Gorilla Sensei put his hands together. Everyone else followed suit.

“”””Thank you for the food!””””

After these words, the contest for the side dishes began. Well, we brought enough so we wouldn’t run out that easily. Everyone freely picked their karaage and other dishes and put them onto paper plates.

Someone was the first to try a bite.

“…Mh!?”

“Oy, what’s wrong?”

“…Try the karaage.”

“Huh, sure… mh!?”

They all fell still after nibbling on their first bite. They seemed lost for words.

Didn’t it taste good?

“I-Is something wrong?”

“Does it taste bad?”

“N-No… on the contrary…” Hoshino muttered as he trembled. “This is better than my mom’s cooking… even as someone who usually doesn’t eat out, I can tell that this is something you’d get in a three-star restaurant.”

“Exactly, that’s how it feels. This doesn’t taste like boxed lunch you’d just get everywhere. It’s closer to food from a restaurant with a month-long waiting list costing you several tens of thousands of Yen…!”

“Thish ish the firsht time I’m eating food thish delishioush… wow~.”

It made me recall when my parents tried my cooking for the first time. They reacted in a similar manner.

“At any rate, it’s great that you like it.”

“Yum! This is crazy yummy!”

“No need to eat this greedily, we got lots more.”

“If we don’t eat it, it’ll get away!”

It was always a joy to have someone call your cooking delicious and then eat it, no matter where, when, or with whom it happened.

As everyone was devouring the lunch we made, Mika gently tapped me on my shoulder.

“What’s wrong?”

“Your karaage is really good Ayumu.”

“Thanks for saying that.”

“But mine isn’t any worse. Say ‘ah’.”

“Ah.”

_Yep, very good._

---

“Hah… hah… ah~…!”

We finished lunch and several more matches were fought, which brought us to what happened right now…

_“One full point.”_

“He did it!”

Shuu had won the finals.

Unsurprisingly, the final opponent was formidable enough to prevent an instant defeat, but it still ended in a decisive victory with Shuu never having anything resembling a close call.

Of the eight club members who’d participated, five made it to the provincial tournament. Obviously, those were the members of the group participating in the team competition.

“Shuu…! Shuu!”

“Hey, Ayumu. Is it just me, or does Rir look like she’s in heat?”

“I thought the same.”

When Shuu won, her heart seemed to be racing wildly, and her eyes looked fiery. She seemed so moved, her eyes were getting moist. She was exuding so much sexual energy, others might assault her if they saw her in that state. That was the reason Mika had been watching over her for some time.

“In any case, you ended up winning as predicted, Shuu.”

“I guess another celebration is in order.”

“S-Same here! I’ll prepare something nice again for you, Shuu!”

“Sure thing.”

+++

# **621 – In Anazumu After the Prefectural Tournament**

“Here we are.”

As always, we made it back to Anazumu without incident. None of us seemed to be missing. Mika and I, Kanata and Sakura, and finally, Shuu and Rir. The whole gang was here.

“First things first, you did great at the prefectural tournament!” I exclaimed.

“Good job, Shuu,” Mika added.

“Congratulations on your victory,” Kanata said.

“You… you were incredible!” Sakura stammered.

Each of us said their piece. Once the tournament had ended, Shuu had practically been showered in praise, but who didn’t enjoy people fussing over one?

“Ha-ha-ha, thank you, really. It only went that well since you came to cheer for me.”

“What are you saying? You didn’t even break a sweat.”

“I-It ain’t that way. Some of my opponents were plenty strong, if you ask me.”

But Shuu had still been overwhelmingly more powerful. In Anazumu, we could do anything we wanted, so we’d celebrate today like last time.

“So, what would you like to eat today?”

“Oh, you’ll be cooking again? In that case, sushi.”

“Sure thing.”

Yesterday, he mostly ate fried foods, so I could tell that he wanted to eat some raw fish in exchange. That was what I’d prepare, then.

“Keep this up and you’ll win the national tournament.”

“Right!”

“Huh? I only just noticed, but what’s with Rir?”

Now that she mentioned it, the one who’d normally be first in line to sing Shuu’s praises hadn’t said a single word.

“If you’re looking for her, she’s here.”

He turned around, showing us his back where we found her clinging to him like a parasite. Come to think of it, all I did see of her earlier were her arms.

“Rir, what are you doing?”

“…Woof, hugging Shuu.”

“She’s been doin’ that since yesterday.”

_Huh… all this time?_

Mika showed a momentary grin. She seemed to have the same thought as I.

“She’s been doing that constantly since you got home?”

“Yes, except during dinner and bath time.”

“Hrm.”

_So, they didn’t take a bath together? Well, Shuu’s mother is usually at home, so they can’t really do something like that._

“So, while we were in my room, she kept huggin’ me.”

“I wonder, was hugging really all you’ve done?”

“Obviously not, at some point he-” Rir replied, her face still buried in Shuu’s back.

“Nope, no telling them that.”

“Mph.”

Before she had a chance to finish her sentence, he quickly peeled her off and hugged her from the front to silence her. But it was already too late with what she managed to blurt out.

“Hey, Mika, these two will be having fun in their room today, won’t they?” I asked teasingly.

“They will. What about us, then?”

“I’m up for it if you are.”

We had this exchange with grins on our faces right in front of Shuu. As for Kanata and Sakura, they were already sick of our charade and had left with a short “we’ll be in our room.”

“…A-About that,” Shuu stammered.

“Yes, I’ll be having a special treat for you today, too,” Rir replied.

“Wasn’t what happened yesterday enough?”

“No, that would mean I did less than last time. We wouldn’t want that, would we?”

I’d never imagined I’d have this kind of conversation with my childhood friends. Well, we were still young.

“Then we better split up and each have our fun, right?”

“Woof! Let’s do that.”

“R-Rir, please don’t go even crazier than usual… nah, don’t go crazy at all.”

Thus, us two couples split up and went to our respective rooms.

“Phew…”

“What’s wrong, Mika?”

“I was just thinking about Rir,” she replied as she created some juice and sat down on the sofa.

“Is there an issue? She seemed as madly in love with Shuu as usual.”

“It was the first time I saw her this excited on the other side… I was wondering if I appear the same when I’m with you, Ayumu.”

Were there ever times when she acted like Rir yesterday? It made me wonder how Kanata and Sakura saw us.

“Well, does it matter that much? As long as we love each other, we’ll be fine.”

“I didn’t expect you to say that. But you’re right, there’s no problem,” she replied with a smile before downing the liquid.

The next moment, her body changed to her 16-year-old appearance.

“Eh-heh-heh, with that said, Ayumu~. Is it time to make out?”

“Yep, it is.”

I also reverted to my older appearance right away. I pulled Mika, who was still sitting on the sofa, by her hand and then drew her close. There was a nice smell on her. Keeping up the flow of things, I picked her up in a princess carry.

_Alright, to the bed as usual and then we’ll-_

⟦Alim, Mika! We have news[1](#easy-footnote-bottom-1-120374)!⟧

For now, I gently lowered Mika to the bed. We silently shot each other a glance before sighing.

Indeed, just as usual.

# **621.5 – Rir’s Reward After the Prefectural Tournament**

“Woof, woof.”

Rir let out moaning sounds as she kept clinging to my back.

On Earth after the tournament was over and we were back home, she kept acting this way. She constantly hugged me, or rather, tried to get me to touch her body. So, I indulged her and groped the parts I loved most about her. I just didn’t expect her to try to cheerfully inform my childhood friends about this.

“Shuu, I love you.”

“Right, I know.”

That was the state she was in. It made me wonder what she had planned this time. Last time, she started with a massage, then did the naked apron, and we finished by having sex like usual.

_The naked apron… to be honest, that one was awesome. If I could, I’d always have her do that one, but I better put that outta my mind for now._

“Rir.”

“Woof, woof~, awoo!”

“Rir…”

I didn’t mind her hugging me, but what was I supposed to do about this?

In any case, Ayumu and Mika warned me that Rir got dangerously aroused when she watched my matches. With their ample experiences of all kinds with men, they were undoubtedly correct when they judged that if anyone with ill intentions saw her at such times, they would assault her. I promised to protect her for the rest of her life, but that was like putting the cart before the horse if she got like this just by watching me.

That said, I couldn’t simply distance myself from it. I had to deal with this.

“Hah… hah… woof?”

“Somethin’ wrong?”

“Ah… I just realized we’re back in our room. I was so focused on you, I never noticed.”

After suddenly regaining her senses, she checked the time. Then, she let go off me… which also meant that the soft sensation was no longer on my back.

“Now, Shuu. What should we do? Will you massage my breasts like you did yesterday?”

“Nah… I’ll refrain for now.”

“Woof? You do realize that I’m up for anything, as long as it’s with you? Just tell me if there’s anything you’d like to do! I was planning to do more than last time, so if you have a request, I’ll go with it!”

“You’re quite eager, huh…?”

“Woof. It’s because I want to make you happy!” she replied with an exquisite smile.

_That ain’t good, I might die from all that cuteness. That alone is enough of a reward._

_Well… since we’re already here…_

“For now, could you give me a massage?”

“Woof, a proper one? Or maybe…”

“A proper one.”

“Leave it to me!”

I could tell that she was implying something lewd with the other massage. She didn’t even have to finish that sentence. Definitely.

“So, what kind of costume should I put on?”

“Huh? A costume?”

“Exactly! I was going to change into something different, like that naked apron last time! What would you like? I could also pick something on random.”

“Uhm…”

_So, she’s goin’ to pick somethin’ either way. She won’t just give up on this, will she?_

“I assume these outfits are all suggestive?”

“Of course. Those are the ones that excite you… right, Shuu? Just tell me if I’m wrong.”

Since I had the chance, I might as well ask something I’d been wondering about. Why she acted so much like an exhibitionist, or whatever you’d call that, around me.

“Rir, whenever we’re doin’ somethin’, you’re always undressin’ and showin’ me your underwear, right?”

“I do. Is that an issue?

“Nah, it’s fine if I’m the only one with you. Rather, I like it when you do that.”

This was the truth. To be honest, if she wore suggestive outfits, or nothing at all, and touched me… that was exactly what I wanted. I never thought I’d turn into such a degenerate.

“Still, aren’t you pushin’ yourself too far in exchange? Just for my sake.”

“In the end, that’s all I can do… I love you!” she replied with glittering eyes full of expectation. “You’re my lover, so my wish to do something for you is stronger than my shame! It does make you happy… doesn’t it?”

It was utterly adorable.

“I see, and you’re not wrong…”

_Why am I so embarrassed when it’s just the two of us? I gotta tell her plainly._

“‘Course it makes me happy… Anyway, for now, come here, Rir.”

“Woof!”

As I spread my arms to avoid the topic, she flung herself onto my chest. I embraced her gently. Things changed a lot ever since we got close. I could feel that keenly.

“Rir, I love you.”

“Woof… I love you, too…”

If she told me that this was my reward, then I’d be satisfied.

“Woof, I’ll give you the massage, then!”

“Ah, right. Please do.”

She kept improved at them. She was probably practicing daily in Anazumu.

“What should I do about my outfit?”

“Just stay as you are. In exchange, I’d love a full-body massage.”

“Woof, understood!”

Part of me was curious what suggestive outfit she’d pick, but this was fine, too. With how things were going, it was highly likely that I’d gaze at her body for hours on end later.
