# **622 – New Information**

“Our apologies for making you come here again… Don’t you seem to be in a poor mood each time we meet?”

After he had contacted Mika and me, we’d undone the transformation into our high schooler selves, and reluctantly made our way to King Rama.

That said, it was necessary to be diplomatic and listen to him, seeing he was our fan. We couldn’t just ignore him. Still, it was undeniable that he had interrupted our precious (or maybe not that precious) alone time.

“That’s not it… you just always seem to have poor timing, Your Majesty…”

“I-Is that so? We apologize.”

_Even so, why does he keep calling us here to discuss his country’s history?_

“To begin with…” I started.

_Hang on. It might be simple to tell him to stop bothering us, but right now, we need the information. It’s only thanks to what he told us that we learned the vajra is on Earth._

“No, it’s nothing.”

“Hm?”

Still, it made me wonder why he kept telling us about this. First it was about the defeat of their evil god and then to recreate the vajra, so…? It felt like I was missing something. Maybe he was trying to look cool by showing off his knowledge, as men often did. Yes, that was probably it. Getting our attention by acting as if he knew something. Though in his case it was less feigning information, and more telling us about the investigation.

“So, what did you learn this time, Your Majesty?”

“We previously told you that the vajra was moved to another world, resulting in the evil god’s destruction, no?”

“Yes, you did.”

“We discovered more information by comparing Our great grandfather’s writings with other literature.”

_Is this related to the vajra? It would be great if we could use it to search for it._

“Why, it was about the vessel the weapon was placed in!”

“Is that all?”

“Hm, is something wrong?”

_The vessel the weapon was placed into… Aren’t ceremonial weapons like that usually just wrapped in cloth? Even if they learned about that…_

“I mean… you’re talking about the vessel it was put into. Isn’t that normal stuff, like the sheath of the Hero’s Sword?”

“You’re not wrong, but this container was everything but normal… There were detailed descriptions of it, which We were about to tell you.”

_What, they actually know the details? He said it’s everything but normal, so it’s probably something rather unusual. I better listen closely._

“So, what kind of vessel was it, then?”

“From what it says, it was a stone statue, crafted by that very Guide.”

“A stone statue, you say?”

_Meaning, if we search the interior of every stone statue on earth, we’ll eventually find it? That sounds tough, but it’s better than having no clue at all, I guess. Well, let’s ask for more details._

“What kind of statue was it?”

“Do you know about the prayer pose used to address the gods?”

“I do.”

There was this foreign religion… Christianity, I think. The way you folded your hands in prayer for that was close to what they did on Anazumu. There were some small, strange differences, though, so you could tell at a glance that it wasn’t the same.

“From what it says, the statue is in this prayer pose.”

“Huh…”

“But it was apparently strangely small for a stone statue. Only the height of a four- or five-year-old child.”

“Hrm.”

_Won’t that narrow down the search quite a bit? A smallish stone statue with its hands folded in prayer._

“Were there any other details?”

“There were. It said that as a finishing touch, it was made to wear a red apron and not a single hair was chiseled into its head.”

“Let me get that straight, it’s completely bald and wearing a red apron?”

“Indeed. We can’t quite imagine it, since there were no drawings.”

_A stone statue… child sized… bald… wearing a red apron… Hang on, couldn’t that be…_

_I should ask Mika._

“Hey, Mika, doesn’t that sound like a Jizou statue?”

“You might be onto something there.”

“Right… but still.”

A few things didn’t fit. Jizou statues usually had their hands in a Japanese style prayer and were in a Buddha pose holding a pewter staff. Were there any such statues with their hands folded in the western style?

“Have we ever seen a Jizou statue in that prayer pose?”

“I’m not sure… hang on?”

Mika suddenly clutched her head.

“What’s wrong?”

“The Jizou statue in our neighborhood is famous, among other things, because it looks different from normal statues, isn’t it?”

“Yes, it is.”

“I’m pretty sure one of those differences is the way its hands are folded…”

_Hang on, did we just realize something huge?_

“Is something wrong, you two? That reminds Us, that very Guide was said to have returned to his world by bestowing some kind of enchantment to the statue.”

_That sounds like the world transfer function of our Jizou statue. Hang on… just one moment… this is starting to sound really fishy._

+++

# **623 – Genten Jizou’s Origins**

“What’s wrong, you two? For your expressions to change that much,” King Rama gently asked, but we didn’t have the leeway to explain it to him right now.

The vajra – the very weapon sealing the evil god – was inside our neighborhood’s Jizou statue. I had been thinking of spending the next few years with Mika slowly searching every small stone statue with hands folded in prayer. This wasn’t what I expected.

“Uhm… ah… No, we’re fine.”

“Right, other than what We just told you, you could apparently remove the statue’s head, which served as a lid!” King Rama continued, likely due to my better-than-usual reaction. “This seemed to frighten Our great grandfather somewhat. Also, before you could remove the head, you had to offer an Anazuman prayer. Well, the religion in another world is likely different, so this seems like quite the stroke of genius of the Guide. It made it even more difficult to break the seal, in the unlikely chance someone would try.”

He wasn’t wrong, the religions on Earth and in Anazumu differed. And it was rather improbable for someone to pray to a Japanese Jizou statue in the manner of Christianity or other western religions. It was well thought out and should offer us some peace of mind.

_Hang on…_

“Hey, Mika. Do you remember that story from Sanada that Shuu told us a few weeks ago?”

“I do, we are probably thinking the same.”

When Rir, who grew up with Anazuman beliefs, offered such a prayer to the statue, something abnormal occurred. And later, according to Sanada, someone removed the statue’s head and placed it next to it. These two occurrences.

“Isn’t that bad.”

“It is… very.”

You couldn’t call this situation anything but catastrophic. It meant that there was a high chance the contents of the statue had already been taken. And just recently, at that.

“That reminds Us, the Guide apparently mentioned that his name was ‘Buke’… Alim, Mika? What’s wrong for you to look so downcast? Was there something about the information We gave you just now?”

“…Uhm… about that… well.”

I could only provide the king with an ambiguous answer. Though you could say that the matter involved his family.

“The way you look tells Us it is anything but normal.”

“I-I’m sorry. Would you mind if we left for today, Your Majesty?”

“…Understood. But if anything comes up, feel free to contact Us. We’ll show you the documents and historical texts We are currently researching.”

“Th-Thank you so much for the offer, Your Majesty!”

I impulsively gripped the king’s hand firmly. If your asked me, people who could infer such things were incredible.

“You may leave, then.”

“Alright! Thank you for your hospitality and ’til another time!”

Mika and I hurriedly broke into a run. While being back at our own residence wouldn’t mean that we could immediately do something, we were still able to put our thoughts in order.

“Could it be that you two… Anyway, We won’t be washing our hands today.”

I heard King Rama mumble something, which I assumed was a goodbye. I put it out of my mind, and we left the castle.

---

“Now, let’s discuss this,” I started.

“Shouldn’t we call Sakura and Kanata?”

“If we involve my brother, he’ll end up seriously pondering it. Let’s hold off asking for help until we gathered our thoughts.”

For now, with the flow of time in Anazumu not being tied to the one of Earth, we had lots of time.

“You mean summing up what we learned today?”

“We now know that our neighborhood’s Jizou statue was made in Anazumu and that the vajra with the sealed evil god was placed into it, but its head was recently removed, which does seem rather suspicious.”

Everything about this was suspicious. Moreover, we had heard that Rir had entered some trance state after performing a prayer and then tried to remove the statue’s head. The fact that the evil god was able to use telepathy or something like it, could mean that it already had regained a lot of power.

In any case.

“If whatever has been placed in the Jizou statue was removed…”

To begin with, it was probably better to assume it was still there until we had a chance to check.

“I wonder who took off the head.”

“If we knew that… Didn’t this super shady guy appear only recently?”

“Yes, that guy.”

It was likely the man wearing the black hood. With his knowledge about both Anazumu and us, he was rather suspect. If someone took what was in the statue, he’d be the prime suspect. His very existence was shady.

“Somehow, we learned a whole lot all at once.”

“It’s all conjectures for now, but my intuition tells me that it’s spot on.”

I felt the same. I did, but it seemed too much at once. Could this pile of bizarre events and coincidences really serve as proof?

“For now, we gathered our thoughts. When do we tell the others?”

“Tomorrow should work. I’m pretty sure Shuu and Rir are busy making out right now.”

“True, we should interrupt them. We know perfectly well how that feels.”

_Now… what should we do from now on? Something as just the two of us?_

“What should we do with the rest of today?”

“Huh? Continue where we left off, obviously.”

“Oh? You want to get back to it, after all that?”

_Surprising. I didn’t expect her to propose such a-_

“This is this and that is that. Doing things in moderation is key.”

“Isn’t it simply that you’re not satisfied yet, Mika?”

“…Yes.”

“Oh, well.”

_Is this really alright…? Well, I guess, since it’s us._

---

**TL notes:**

I’ve complained on several occasions about the author proving unable to surprise their audience or spoiling possible reveals way too early. This is probably the first reveal that doesn’t come out of nowhere, and had foreshadowing for several volumes now without things being spoiled. I’ll be hopeful for now and interpret this as a sign of improvement in the writing.

# **624 – The Opposite of Being Spirited Away**

“Good morning, everyone! There’s a reason we called you here.”

“I’m sure you wouldn’t have if there wasn’t one, Bro.”

It was the following day, and Mika and I had called the others first thing in the morning. Shuu and Rir likely had a lot of fun yesterday, seeing how close they were glued to each other. Mika and I obviously also had our fill and acted affectionately. Even Sakura was hugging Kanata’s arm. Indeed, none of us three couples didn’t act somewhat clingy.

_Why, I don’t have to time to be thinking about that._

“Well, we called you here since something catastrophic happened just yesterday.”

“Huh… what did you and Ayu-nii do, Big Sis?”

“You didn’t turn traitor to the country, did you?”

“Not at all, we didn’t do anything, alright? This is about the evil god.”

The expressions of everyone who’d just been joking turned serious. Especially Shuu, who’d once witnessed Surtr killing Rir, was wearing a rare, puzzled look. It couldn’t be helped.

“So, what exactly happened?”

“Nothing has come from it yet… I’m not sure how to put it. In any case, let me tell you what we did yesterday.”

“Alright.”

---

“…Seriously?

“Yes, seriously.”

Shuu was giving a strained smile while he was sweating bullets. From his look, he still seemed to be hoping that we were playing a prank on him.

“…I mean, I did assume there was some connection to the Jizou statue. To think it was containing such a secret.”

“No way, was Rir seriously on the verge of bein’ possessed back then!? That was a close call…” Shuu commented as he drew his girlfriend closer. “I ain’t gonna let that happen again.”

“Woof…?”

The wolf girl seemed to have question marks over her head for a moment, but then narrowed her eyes, likely in satisfaction at being pulled close to her boyfriend.

“But didn’t you, Mika-nee, and Shuu tell us some time ago that the head of the statue was removed, Bro?”

“Exactly. And then this man in black started showing up, messing with us.”

“…Hm~.”

Kanata was thinking. Meanwhile, Rir raised her hand to ask something.

“To begin with, I haven’t even the slightest idea why that statue was placed there. You mentioned some history behind it, but what exactly is it?”

“The statue reminds of the mysterious appearance of a samurai’s son,” Kanata explained. “It is said that it was donated by a passing sculptor, several years after the boy’s disappearance.”

“Several years later… and they never found the child?”

“Apparently.”

“What a sad story.” Rir’s ears drooped dejectedly. But they immediately stood up again and she continued with another question. “But why would some passerby donate a statue… a Jizou statue? Moreover, one with such a dangerous item from this world in it.”

“Oh, you’re thinking of the same, Rir?” Kanata wondered.

“Woof, There’s only one conclusion.”

_Huh, are those two suddenly on the same wavelength?_

Still, they weren’t wrong. A man suddenly appearing and putting down a Jizou statue filled with something dangerous was awfully suspicious. In the very place someone disappeared… a stranger later delivered an item related to Anazumu.

Thinking of it, it was pretty much like a kidnapping when Sages were summoned. And when it happened, they were erased from any records and memories. But back in the era when Jizou statues were placed around Japan, the disappearance of a single child wouldn’t have been that unnatural. It would have been easy to adjust the story. Even without erasing the memories of people.

_I get it, that’s the conclusion those two reached._

“So, what you’re trying to say is that the one who brought the statue… was the son who disappeared?”

“You got it, Bro. It looks like everyone did.”

When I looked around, I had to agree with him. I thought I’d figured it out right after Kanata and Rir, but it looked like we all got it at the same time. How disappointing.

“But why would he look like an adult if only a few years passed?” Sakura asked. “It wasn’t like that with us.”

“Well, it’s hard to say in our case since only a few months passed, but if gods can freely adjust things like they please, as they did with Rir and Mr. Mitsuo, it doesn’t seem that impossible.”

It took us only a few minutes of discussing yesterday’s events to make so much progress. It was the right call to rely on my brother, he just kept surpassing me.

“In that case, is the man wearing the black hood also a samurai?” Sakura wondered. “He keeps saying nonsensical things.”

“Nonsensical…? Oh, I get what you mean. It’s too early to tell, but we can’t rule out the possibility. He could also be the evil god.”

It was fun to see them come to their interpretations. Being able to leave everything to a gifted younger sibling wasn’t a bad thing.

+++

# **625 – If the Revival Happened on Earth**

“Honestly, we can’t ignore the possibility that the evil god has already been resurrected and is simply hiding, either. We should keep all those options in mind.”

“Woof, that’s true!”

Kanata managed to wrap things up nicely after some consideration. He’d probably had all these possibilities in mind already.

That one of them…

“Woof, that leaves the question what we are supposed to do if the evil god revives over there, where we can’t use our abilities and stats to fight back.”

“Did you think of something, Rir?”

“No, that’s not what I meant. I just have something personal I’d like to ask Shuu. It doesn’t concern this conversation.”

“Me? What’s up?”

Indeed, there was the option where the evil god came back to life on Earth and wreaked havoc. Kanata had theorized that skills might become available at such a moment, but there was no guarantee. If they did, we could fight normally using Item Master to prevent casualties, damages, and the public finding out about it (especially our identities). The problem was if they didn’t.

If we were stuck with only a few skills available – none of them magic – the situation might be hopeless. Kanata’s impression of fighting Surtr one on one when Shuu had been possessed, was that a nuke wouldn’t have been enough. Well, they would still cause damage, so if fired in rapid succession, a victory might be possible, but that would devastate Japan. In other words, we’d all die.

That would simply be meaningless.

“If a scenario where all hope is lost came to pass… would you be willing to die with me?”

“What? Uhm… well, ‘course I would. Honestly, I wasn’t thinkin’ of dyin’ or anythin’, but we’ll at least be together until the end.”

“Woof~…”

Rir seemed awfully happy.

“What about us, Ayumu?” Mika jumped on the bandwagon, pressing me.

“That’s obvious. I’d hate to be the one to survive if you died… It’d would make me want to die, too. Well, the best would be if we both lived on together.”

“Eh-heh-heh, that’s true!”

From an outside perspective, it probably seemed as if we had a carefree discussion about world-ending scenarios, but at the end of the day we each wanted to save the people close to us. The ideal was still to solve this without a single casualty, though.

“Hah… Somehow, even if we’re trying to have a serious conversation, it always turns to our relationships…”

“Right. But how does it actually look, Kanata? I know you’d struggle until the very end, but what if things really fell apart?”

Sakura seemed curious about my brother’s estimation, after seeing the other two couples’ happy reactions. She looked serious when she asked her question.

“Oh… I’ll save you, Sakura, no matter what it takes.”

“Uhm…”

“Is what I’d like to say, but I can tell you wouldn’t be happy about that. My answer is the same as those of the others; let’s stick together until the end, alright?”

“Yeah…!”

The serious atmosphere instantly changed into one of affection. If love really saved the world, then how often had it happened already?

“Woof, in any case, sorry for bringing that up! Did you have something else you wanted to discuss?” Rir apologized shortly later after coming back to her senses.

“Nothing in particular. We can only see what happens when we’re back on Earth.”

“Hm~, if you ask me, the resurrection already happened, but for some reason, nothing else occurred… or rather, the evil god doesn’t feel like doing something.”

“If you say so, Big Sis, it might be true, which is scary by itself.”

Mika’s eerily accurate intuition. If she was right, then things might stay peaceful for some time.

“In any case, everythin’ depends on our skills. To put it bluntly, if the evil god appears on Earth and we can use ’em, it’ll be easy to save the world. And if we can’t, we might as well give up.”

“Yes, it’s rather straightforward.”

It was. Everything boiled down to whether we could use our skills when our enemy appeared. According to Kanata’s theory, since Earth and Anazumu were starting to overlap, it was possible that magic became useable the moment the evil god appeared. We could only hope that he was correct.

“From now on, we should stay in close contact and if the man wearing the black hood appears, we ask him the questions we worked out today. Let’s keep that in mind no matter what we do.”

“””Yes!”””

_Now, will the evil god even show up? I have a feeling it’s going to happen. But I’d rather have it sooner than later… Right, I better ask Mika what her gut says._

“Hey, Mika, when do you think the evil god is going to show up?”

“A few days before our exams, I guess.”

“Meaning next week, huh…”

Well, it would certainly convenient if she was right, since that week wouldn’t overlap with the finale of Shuu’s tournament.

+++

# **626 – At Night, at the Jizou Statue – 1**

“Morning, Mika.”

“Good morning, Ayumu.”

We had just come back from Anazumu, but there were things to discuss.

“So, are we really going for it?”

“Not sure. I’ll ask during breakfast.”

The other day, in Anazumu together with Kanata and the others, we had laid bare the Jizou statue’s secrets and discussed things. After Rir brought up the question of what we’d do if we were to face our ends, to which we had reacted with assertions to stay together until the end, Kanata had instructed us in what we should do from this point on.

_“Ayumu~, breakfast is ready!”_ I heard my mom shout.

It sounded like she had made breakfast. On that note, after finding out how skilled Kanata and I were at cooking, she’d been asking one of us to make breakfast or dinner every other day. It was one of my strengths, so I didn’t mind.

Moreover, Mika was making boxed lunch for me every day, recently. The whole “lunch box made by one’s loving spouse” thingy (just as Mom made Dad’s lunch). Mom said this alone did a great deal to keep the relationship steady[1](#easy-footnote-bottom-1-121035), which was good to know.

“I’m coming~! See you later, Mika.”

“Same.”

She leaned out of the window, gave me a kiss on my cheek, and then withdrew to her room. Following her example, I also descended from the second floor to the living room.

“Morning, Mom!”

“Good morning, Ayumu. Have some breakfast, will you?”

“Sure!”

“Morning, Bro.”

“Morning.”

“Oh, Ayumu. Good morning.”

“Morning, Dad.”

How many more times would I wish someone a good morning today? This was already the fourth time, though that happened every day.

“So, Bro, are we still up? For tonight.”

“Yep, we are. But the thought of incurring divine punishment is scary.”

“Not like we have a choice. It’s the only way to verify it…”

“Grr… Hmph.”

Indeed, just as Kanata had said, we were going to visit the Jizou statue at night, remove its head, and check what was inside it. With everything that happened, it was more likely that the vajra had already been taken, but seeing was believing and we’d never know for sure unless we looked.

“What are you talking about?”

“Oh, we were thinking of going out for a bit today after dinner, Mom. There’s something we’d like to verify.”

“Something for which you have to leave the house after dinner…?”

“Exactly. Shuu’s coming too, so there’s no reason to worry.”

“He will? Alright, then. Are you going to meet up somewhere else to study?”

“Well, not exactly, but I guess it’s close enough.”

Just from the words, it sounded like utter nonsense, but my brother managed to pull it off with the way he talked and acted. I knew I could count on him.

On another note, Shuu didn’t leave the house that often anymore at this point. We were also planning to have Rir wait some ways away. It might be dangerous for her to get close to the statue. That said, if Shuu wasn’t around us, there was the risk of us getting kidnapped, so he couldn’t stay with her. He alone (at least according to Kanata’s estimations) was enough to take down several armed terrorists.

“The food was great!”

“Thank you for saying that. Go and get changed.”

“Alright.”

I went to my room on the second floor and started to change. At exactly the same time, Mika was doing the same.

“Ah, you’re back Ayumu. So? Did your parents give you permission?”

“Kanata gave them a simplified explanation, which got them to accept.”

“That’s very much like him. We said that we’d go to Shuu’s house to study with Rir and would eat dinner there.”

“Oh… I should’ve said that, too. We’ll be eating dinner at home.”

_I messed that one up. The thought of eating out never crossed my mind._

“Oh, well. It’s been a while since it was just Sakura and me on our own.”

“Alright, sorry for not thinking of it.”

Afterwards, we got changed without further incident (at the point where I got back to my room, she’d already been mostly dressed, so I unfortunately didn’t get to see her in her underwear) and left the house.

“Alright, let’s go!”

“Why don’t we pass the statue on our way there? We could do a preliminary check before we meet there tonight.”

“Alright.”

We held hands as always and made our way to the statue. It was so close that we got there in no time at all, while being teased by our neighbors about being so affectionate.

“Do you notice any signs?”

“Nothing I can see… Even the limited version of the Detection skill doesn’t pick up anything.”

“…I see. What about the statue and its peculiarities?

I took a closer look at it. It had been years since I scrutinized it that intently. It definitely was different from normal Jizou statues. It was praying with its fingers interlinked, not just its palms pressed against each other. There were several other differences from the norm, but listing them all would’ve taken too long.

After folding our hands as customary, we took each other’s hands again and walked off.

“I wonder if this will work.”

“I thought we’d encounter the man in the black hood here, but it didn’t happen…”

“We’ve got plenty of time, but let’s be off.”

“Alright.”

We made our way to school.

#### **Footnotes:**

1. The original is rather ambivalent and doesn’t specify “relationship” here, so it might simply mean that it makes “things” easier/more comfortable

+++

# **627 – At Night, at the Jizou Statue – 2**

“Good morning, everyone!”

“Good morning!”

Mika and I arrived at our classroom after finding the usual (though somewhat reduced) pile of love letters in our shoe cubbies. It was crazy that people still kept leaving them there.

“Morning, Mika,” Sanada spoke up. “I’m sure you guys know already, right?”

“Good morning, Sana,” Mika greeted her. “Are you talking about Shuu’s double victory at the prefectural tournament? We were there and saw it in person.”

“That’s the one. I’m sure it will be the talk of the school today. I’ve been telling everyone since yesterday.”

“Heh, I can’t say I’m surprised.”

If she had told everyone she knew about Shuu’s victories in both the individual and team competition, then it was likely that the whole school was already in on it.

“Isn’t that crazy? Like, seriously crazy?”

“It totally is.”

“Hm? What’s going on?”

Several boys from our class grew noisy as they looked at something on their smartphones. That made me curious.

“Oh, Ayumu. We were watching a video of Hino’s fight in the finals yesterday. Sanada sent it to us.”

_Hang on, did she also come to watch the tournament? She’s quite elusive and unpredictable. I never even noticed she was there._

“I do luchador style wrestling at the gym, so I can tell. It’s crazy just how strong Hino is.”

“It’s insane how even the last fight ends in an instant.”

“Well, it’s Shuu. He makes it possible.”

As the talk about Shuu picked up, the door to the classroom opened with a clatter. My muscular friend and Rir entered.

“Oh, good morning, Mika, Sanada. Huh? Did something happen, everyone?”

“Mornin’, you two. What’s with this atmosphere?”

Shuu looked confused as everyone’s attention turned to him.

“Good morning,” Sanada spoke up. “Well, I’ve simply been spreading the word about your double victory at the prefectural tournament since yesterday. I even attached a video, heh-heh-heh.”

“Are you serious…?”

At the same time as Shuu showed a somewhat displeased smile, everyone pressed in on him at once.

“That was awesome! Keep going like this and you’ll win the national tournament!”

“You’ll be going to the Olympics, right? Next year, I mean!”

“R-Right, I was plannin’ to win the national competition… but whether I go to the Olympics depends on exams.”

“You can do it, Hino!”

“We’ll be rooting for you!”

“Th-Thanks, guys.”

It looked like the harem king had become popular with both boys and girls.

---

“How were the Mapo glass noodles[1](#easy-footnote-bottom-1-121037)? Did they taste good?”

“They were so good, I’ll never be able to eat them at a restaurant again. You have somewhere else to be, right? See you later… and take care.”

“We will! Let’s go, Kanata.”

“We’ll be off.”

Kanata and I left the house. It was 8 pm. Normally, you’d see many passersby in the city even at this time, but this was a residential area and close to a Jizou statue rumored to cause strange phenomena, so there were barely any people. Though pedestrian traffic was normal during the daytime.

Either way, we arrived at our destination as I was lost in thought. There were already two cute visitors there.

“Hey there, Mika, Sakura!”

“Hi, Ayumu!”

“What did the two of you eat for dinner?”

“Hamburgers.”

They told us they’d be eating out, so that was apparently what they’d settled on. I hadn’t eaten at any of the fast-food restaurants in a while. I occasionally craved that kind of fatty food, whether you could call it delicious or not.

“Looks like we’re only missing Shuu…”

“There he comes. Together with Rir.”

The two of them had arrived with perfect timing. From where I was standing, I could vaguely see a girl with white hair peeking around a corner three houses away. Unless there was a haunting in the area, this had to be Rir.

“I can see Rir, that means we’re all here.”

“Okay. Let’s start, then.”

“Yeah.”

_Alright, this is getting scarier and scarier._

“Kanata, we’re all set.”

“…Yes. If you would, Bro.”

I gave a Japanese style prayer, apologized profusely, and then grabbed the statue’s head. Even though the stone should’ve been heavy, I could feel it shift easily. That moment, I remembered fixing the statue back in the day. I wondered how it looked back then, but I couldn’t remember looking inside.

“Hng… there. Huh?”

I finally managed to get the head off. But all I could see was stone without an opening anywhere.

“There’s nothing?”

“Huh? How weird.”

“Then let’s put it back and this time use the Anazuman style prayer.”

“Alright.”

I very carefully placed the heavy head where it had been and then performed the other kind of prayer. The moment I did, the atmosphere changed somehow. I could tell that it was completely different, as if there was some kind of pressure.

“I-I’ll take it off, alright?”

“A-Ayumu… should I help you?”

“I’m good…”

I put my hand on the statue’s head again. It somehow felt lighter than before. And once it was off… an aperture had appeared where there hadn’t been one before.

#### **Footnotes:**

1. Mapo (麻婆), likely the shortened version of [Mapo Tofu](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mapo_tofu), is a Chinese dish with tofu in spicy sauce. I assume they eat that together with glass noodles here.

+++

# **628 – Empty**

“There’s nothing in the aperture, but… I guess we can assume the vajra was in there?”

“Probably.”

The gaping hollow in the statue’s neck was empty. It felt like having the contents of a treasure chest turn out a huge disappointment.

“So, as we feared, the vajra is already…”

“It’s too early to give up! At least that’s what I’d like to say as usual, but we don’t have any clues…”

If even my brother was at a loss, then I didn’t have anything to contribute.

“Uhm, does that mean the evil god… has come back to life?”

“Not necessarily, Sakura. Remember, the other evil gods needed to fulfill some conditions to possess people to fight. If this one hasn’t met those requirements…”

“Now that you mention it, the first evil god we fought could only possess someone from the Mephilad lineage.”

Indeed, we might still have some peace of mind if that was the case. That is, if this evil god had some conditions to take over someone.

“In that case, we’ll have to narrow down these conditions first.”

“Do you have any idea, Kanata?”

“Let’s see… simply put, I can think of two.”

_Two possibilities. Oh, could those be…_

“You’re thinking of either relatives of King Rama or the one designated as the guide, don’t you?”

“You got it. If it’s the former then we don’t have to worry for some time, but if it’s the latter, we’re in trouble.”

Kanata looked serious. I decided to ask him why the latter would be an issue, though I already had a hunch.

“Why would that be so?”

“Come on, if we go over everything we’ve been talking about so far, then the samurai’s son became the guide in Anazumu and then returned here, didn’t he? In other words, the chance of a guide being on Earth is much higher.”

He was right, this sounded like trouble. Thinking back… Samaeyl did possess the corpse of Karua’s mother. If this evil god was able to take over a corpse and the one who took the vajra were to bring it to the corpse of the warrior who’d been spirited away, it would be checkmate[1](#easy-footnote-bottom-1-121059). The evil god would be resurrected on Earth.

“When was the last time a guide was nominated?”

“Ah, Mika and I talked about that with King Rama.”

“Now that you mention it, we did… Nothing big seems to have happened, so let’s call Shuu and Rir over so they can join the discussion. Once they’re here, could you tell us again in detail?”

“Sure thing.”

---

“Woof~… Woof…”

“You fine…? Guess you are.”

“Woof!”

They hesitantly joined us. Kanata then gave them a concise version of what we had discussed so far.

“Still, it’s good nothin’ happened to Rir.”

“Woof, does that mean it was the vajra that controlled my body and not the statue?”

“Possibly.”

It was a reasonable conclusion. It made more sense that it was caused by the seal on the evil god in the vajra starting to come undone, rather than the statue itself.

“Anyway, Bro, could you inform us about the things King Rama told you so far? You only mentioned it in broad strokes so far.”

“Sure, I’ll do that.”

I told them everything the king had explained to us in as much detail as I could remember. Well, with Mika’s memory being a lot better than mine, I relied on her help for most parts.

“Woof, he made someone the guide on a whim?”

“Well, you can never tell what people with careless dispositions are gonna do,” Shuu replied. “Was the Bufura Kingdom okay, back then?”

I wondered about that too, but they probably had been. Or maybe, like in Yggdrasil right now, the other politicians made it work somehow.

“Say, Bro. The previous Guide was active around 100 years ago. He was an otherworlder from Anazumu’s perspective, his specialty was performances, he had an intense longing to return to his homeland, and he later moved to the Mephilad Kingdom following a clue… did I get that right?”

“I think so. Was there anything else, Mika?”

“No, that’s what Ayumu and I were told.”

Kanata put his finger to his chin. Not a moment later, he turned pale. It was unusual for him to be rattled to this extent by anything unrelated to Sakura. In other words…

“Did you think of something?”

“I did… or rather, it answered something.”

“I knew you could do it! So, what is it?”

He slowly opened his mouth but hesitated, as if being afraid to put it into words. Just what did he realize?

“Are you alright? If it’s hard to say, just whisper it to me and I’ll relay it to the others.”

“No, that’s not it… what do I do…”

“Kanata…? Are you really alright?”

Sakura rubbed the boy’s back as he was taking deep breaths. He really must’ve come to some conclusion. And he clearly had trouble putting it into words.

_He’s still only an eight grader… maybe I put to much of a burden on him._

Sakura stopped rubbing his back and gently hugged him from behind. He looked like he had made up his mind and opened his mouth again.

“Well… I’m mostly certain at this point… I mean, I figured out who the previous Guide was. Do you want to know?”

“Yeah.”

“No matter how you look at it, it’s Mr. Mitsuo.”

---

**TL notes:**

If there ever was a chapter demonstrating how much Alim and Mika’s supposed intelligence (which was emphasized again and again by the school they’re attending being one of the most demanding) simply not being there, it’s this one.

They went and pretty much confirmed that Mephistophales is the Guide less than 20 chapters ago. They should have realized the trouble they are in the moment Kanata brought up the chance of there being a Guide on Earth, but… nothing.

#### **Footnotes:**

1. The original is 積み (“pile”) which I assume is a typo and meant to be 詰み (“checkmate”)

+++

# **629 – Close to Giving Up**

“…Really?”

“I mean, it’s obvious when you think about it.”

According to Kanata’s hypothesis, Mr. Mitsuo was pretty much guaranteed to be the Guide. First, 100 years ago was a period where he was supposedly asleep. Next were his performance skills – likely circus techniques – and finally the fact that he went to the Mephilad Kingdom. With this, it was pretty much certain. I mean, it was just as he theorized.

Just why didn’t I think of that? At the time, it didn’t seem urgent, so I didn’t try to catalogue all the information King Rama gave us. I wasn’t nearly as smart as my brother, but if we went simply by IQ, then I should’ve been several dozens of points above the average. Enough to join an organization limited to people with high IQs… Before I started to study in Anazumu, I managed above average grades at school while mostly playing video games and putting in barely any effort. I was an idiot.

“Of all the possibilities, it had to be the absolute worst.”

“True, since right now…”

“The circus performs in this area. Now of all things… It couldn’t have been any worse… Woof~.”

The dread Kanata had displayed earlier spread to the others. Indeed, this was the worst case.

_Why did it end up like this… hang on… on second thought, isn’t this mostly my fault? I was the one who sent Mr. Mitsuo back to Earth, and if I had listened more closely to King Rama, we might’ve been able to take various measures earlier._

“Sorry, everyone. I’m truly sorry.”

“Huh? Why do you say that, Ayumu?”

“Uhm… this is largely my fault. That the worst possible situation came to pass… After all-”

I apologized for what I saw as my failings. My reckless actions led to this situation, so I had to repent for them.

“But most of that was unavoidable, Bro. It’s in the past now and there aren’t many people in the first place who are able to listen seriously to what amounts to someone’s bragging or to abandon a fellow countryman who wants to return to his home.”

“I’m sorry…”

“Geez… it’s not like it’s all your fault,” Mika added as she caressed my head.

“Still… we can’t do anything as we are if the evil god has come back to life. Magic is unusable and we definitely can’t pull out secret moves that leave craters in the ground just by punching. Even if the few skills we can use in our daily life would make us look like superheroes to normal people… they only go so far. They wouldn’t get us anywhere with a monster on the level of an evil god. I estimate more than an 80% chance of it having resurrected at this point.”

I couldn’t even complain about this estimation since it seemed sound.

“Maybe an evil god would be just as restricted as we are, here?” Shuu interjected.

“I can’t say at this point, but if that was the case, human weapons might suffice to take it down.”

“But if it resurrected here, this whole area might turn into a war zone.”

It was true, the possibility of the evil god being limited in power couldn’t be discounted. But with Kanata not giving the idea much thought, he probably thought it unlikely. After all, our enemy was a deity.

“Hah… what should we do?”

“Hm… what indeed.”

Sakura, likely sensing Kanata, who was usually so determined, being in such low spirits, took the boy’s hand and gave him a hug. He stopped his monological musings and met her eyes.

“If the evil god has already come back to life and we have nothing left but to wait for our ends, Sakura…”

“What then?”

“Won’t you marry me?”

The sudden proposal took not only Sakura but all of us by surprise.

“We can’t, we’re only 14, right?”

“No, it should be possible if we claim we’re already engaged and put in an application at the public office.”

“I… I guess…” Sakura concluded after thinking for a bit. “Alright, but only if the worst comes to pass.”

“Woo-hoo, thank you.”

“I-If we really do that… uhm, we’ll do more than just kissing and cuddling… I love you, Kanata.”

The two of them were full on in affection mode, lost in their own world. Being able to act like this even in such a situation; it was just like us.

“…Should we do the same?”

“Let’s,” I replied to Mika’s proposal.

It might be for the best if things played out according to Kanata’s conclusion. That way, even if we died, we’d be united with our loved ones forever.

“Woof…”

“They’re right, let’s do the same.”

In the end, all of us were planning to do that. Well, it wasn’t exactly surprising.

“Still, we could escape to Anazumu, so it probably won’t happen.”

_Now that he mentions it. But then we can’t have a wedding here._

“Plus, I was half joking so far. Bro, please contact Mr. Mitsuo at once. I doubt there’s a performance this late.”

“Alright.”

_Huh, so he was joking? It’s often hard to tell if my brother is serious or joking._

_Anyway, I should call Mr. Mitsuo._

+++

# **630 – A Phone Call and Roasted Potatoes**

_“Aichou speaking. What are you calling for?”_

“Hello, it’s Joujou. I am speaking with Mr. Mitsuo, correct?”

_“Joujou_[1](#easy-footnote-bottom-1-121063)_…? Oh, you’re Mr. Ayumu. How can I help you?”_

Judging from his voice, nothing had changed about him. It didn’t seem as if he had any connection to the vajra on Earth.

“Uhm… I’m calling to verify a few things.”

_“To verify something? Is this related to Anazumu?”_

“Yes.”

Previously, Mr. Mitsuo told us that he didn’t remember anything from 100 years ago. Though it would be good to verify this once more.

“Just to make sure, you still don’t recall anything from 100 years ago?”

_“No… If I had to say, all that I remember is the shock caused by the transfer.”_

“I see.”

_So, he doesn’t remember anything, after all._

“Bro, ask him about the vajra next,” Kanata whispered into my ear.

That was fine, but still…

“Alright, alright, but could you guys stand a bit further from me?”

“We have to be this close if we want to hear what he says[2](#easy-footnote-bottom-2-121063).”

“Hm~.”

_Isn’t all five of them crowding around me to listen to the phone call a bit much? It’s still stifling hot, although winter is only one or two weeks away. I guess it can’t be helped. I’ll put up with the heat and continue my phone call._

“I-In that case, don’t you know anything about the vajra Indra, the sealing tool of the Guide?”

_“Is this vajra from Indian mythology? No… I can’t say I remember anything.”_

It sounded like he still didn’t recall those things. I was also convinced that he was the Guide, but… if he couldn’t remember anything, he wasn’t of any help.

“Ask him next about the Jizou statue, Bro.”

“Alright. Do you know anything about Genten Jizou, the famous statue in this city?”

_“Gen… ten? No, nothing comes to mind.”_

“It looks the same as the Jizou statue I used to send you back to Earth, Mr. Mitsuo.”

_“Oh, that one. That kind of statue… now that you mention it-“_

That seemed to have caused a reaction. I was curious what it reminded him of, but I missed it due to someone else making noise.

“Roasted sweet potatoes! Get them while they’re hot!”

_“-is what I think…”_

“Gah…”

“Bro, ask him to repeat that.”

I didn’t expect the sound of someone selling sweet potatoes would make it impossible to hear the crucial part at this hour. On the other hand, this _was_ a residential area in late fall, so people selling them would obviously come here. Though I hadn’t eaten any so far, this season.

“Uhm, excuse me. There was a baked potato seller making noise. Could you repeat that once more? The part about the Jizou statue.”

_“Of course, it’s no problem. What I was saying-“_

“Roasted sweet potatoes! The best you’ll ever find!”

_“Roasted sweet potatoes! The best you’ll ever find!”_

“God damn it!”

_What’s with this awful timing?_

The sound was even louder now. It made me feel like puffing out my cheeks. No choice, I had to ask him to repeat that once more.

“I’m really sorry, could you…”

“Wait a moment, Bro,” Kanata stopped me.

_What now?_

“What’s wrong?”

“It feels like there’s something off. Let me try something.”

“Uhm?”

Kanata looked uncharacteristically serious. Was I the only one who hadn’t noticed that something was wrong? Rir and Shuu were also surveying the area restlessly.

“I’m going to shout loudly for a moment. Cover your ears.”

“Huh, what?”

“Hah…”

My brother took a deep breath and then let out a shout.

“Woah!! That shocked me!!!”

_“Woah! That shocked me!”_

“Huh?”

The moment Kanata shouted about his surprise for whatever reason, you could hear his shout come back in a smallish voice from some distance away.

_In other words…_

“Kanata, I’ll search over there,” Rir said.

“I’ll also go look,” Shuu agreed.

“…S-Same here,” Sakura added.

“Ayumu, keep talking so Mr. Mitsuo doesn’t escape.”

Everyone was suddenly moving. It looked like I was the only one who didn’t notice what was going on. Maybe it was one of those things you didn’t notice when they were happening to you.

“Yep, just like Mika-nee said, please keep talking, Bro. I’ll search over there. Let’s go, everyone.”

At Kanata’s words, everyone was about to rush off. Only, to immediately come to a halt. As for the reason…

“Well… you found me, so I guess I have no choice.”

Mr. Mitsuo, in his clown make-up, emerged from the shadow of the opposite house. He wore what looked like a pitch-black coat.

#### **Footnotes:**

1. He says “nariue” in the original, which I assume is an error.

2. They all know him, so why not put him on speaker?

+++

# **631 – The Time has Come**

“”…!?””

The way he showed up was ridiculously shady. He looked like he had as Long-Heart. Meeting a clown wearing a black coat at night in a residential area did evoke nothing but dread. The two men in our group – Shuu and Kanata – at once stepped in front of the other four (including me) to protect us.

“Oh dear, please don’t mind me that much.”

“…Why are you here, Mr. Mitsuo?” Kanata asked the grinning clown without showing any fear.

“Why… who knows?”

“It’s obviously no coincidence. What’s your aim here?” Shuu added.

_Wow, the two of them are acting quite cool._

“My aim, you ask?”

“Exactly, there’s a lot we want to know, but first things first.”

The two of them were still standing in front of us. Mr. Mitsuo’s shadiness was off the charts; at this point, he no longer seemed sane.

“You’re right, I came here to meet you… Is that not something I’m allowed to do?”

“So, you know what we were trying to do earlier?”

Kanata glared at the clown. The latter’s expression was unchanged, still grinning.

“I assume you came here to do something with the Jizou statue we were talking about earlier.”

“…Yes, you’re correct. But how do you know about this place and managed to come here just as we were meeting?”

“Couldn’t it have been divine guidance?”

He kept up the clown antics to the bitter end.

_Just what’s going on? This is way too suspicious._

Kanata turned for just an instant, checking on is, before looking back at the clown.

“I see, divine guidance, then.”

“Why indeed, it was.”

“That might be a sudden question, but could you put up the hood of your jacket?” Kanata suddenly asked, likely having an idea.

“Huh?”

What was my brother planning?

“Does this satisfy you?”

“”””…!?””””

I was wrong, my brother hadn’t been trying something, he had come to a realization. Or rather, Mr. Mitsuo was… he was…

“So, the man who followed us recently… was you, Mr. Mitsuo, was it?”

“A most excellent deduction.”

“…What!?”

The clown’s voice had suddenly changed, explaining Sakura’s exclamation of shock. It was a voice I’d heard somewhere before.

“Don’t tell me, you’re the man in the black hood?”

“Surprised? Didn’t I tell you when we parted that we’d meet again? I’m sure I said this to you all.”

This meant… the mysterious man’s true identity was Mr. Mitsuo. That said, the atmosphere around him had changed way too much. It was like his earlier clownish manners had done a one-eighty, somehow changing to those of a strict samurai.

“What was the big idea, buggin’ us like that?”

“You’re wondering where I was going with that? I can’t answer that question.”

In the first place, I had never heard him talk like this. Even if he was in a pinch or hurry, he usually talked in a polite manner[1](#easy-footnote-bottom-1-121110). He was acting like a different person. It didn’t feel as if everything since I first met him in Anazumu was an act for some calculated goal. Maybe we were asking the wrong questions.

“Sorry, Kanata, could I do this?”

“…Alright.”

My brother obediently stepped back.

_Now then…_

“Say, Mr. Mitsuo.”

“What is it?”

“I mean, you’re not Mr. Mitsuo in the first place, are you? I only gave you my full name and contact details after we got talking recently, so why would you act as if you know us from years ago?”

I was trying to get to the bottom of this, by bringing up the hooded man’s strange nostalgia about us. There were simply too many contradictions.

“I see, it seems like I answered Kanata’s questions a bit too honestly.”

“Yep, you have… so, who are you?” I tried to go straight to the point.

The clown (or not) only sighed exasperatedly.

“Who do you think I am?”

“I don’t know, that’s why I’m asking you.”

“You’ve got a point. In that case, let me show you something that might give you a hint,” he replied, before starting to rummage in his satchel.

What he finally brought out… was a vajra with lavish decorations.

No, no way. No matter how I looked at it, that was Indra. I could tell since I created a reproduction of it before.

“Am I right to assume that you gathered today to look for this?”

“You are, we did… Why do you have it!?”

“No other reason than taking it the normal way.”

He had the vajra, which meant…!

_Could it be… that we’re in awfully big trouble?_

#### **Footnotes:**

1. In the original, Mitsuo usually talks in the normal polite (desu/masu) form, while the man in black doesn’t, though this sadly isn’t noticeable in my translation

+++

# **632 – Too Late**

“Ha-ha, the very worst possibility we predicted,” Kanata muttered.

Even I understood. The fact that Mr. Mitsuo, who was likely the Guide, already had the vajra, in which the evil god had been sealed, in his possession, was incredibly bad. No, “bad” wasn’t enough to describe the gravity of our situation. With how even his memories had changed, there was only one possibility…

“Mr. Mitsuo, do you know what this vajra is?”

“That should be obvious, it’s the tool of the Guide.”

“So, you do know…”

He knew that much. If this was really him, then he shouldn’t have had this knowledge.

“Hey, Kanata…” Sakura started. “Could it be that he’s…”

“It’s probably what you’re thinking. I had several plans in mind, but at this point it’s already too late. Everyone, get ready to flee at a moment’s notice.”

There was an incredible tension in the air. Everyone understood at this point. The clown in front of us wasn’t Mr. Mitsuo, but a fiendish being.

“What, there’s no need to be this vigilant.”

“We obviously are,” Shuu boldly replied. “After all… you’re the evil god, aren’t ya?”

“As you say, Shuu. Well, you’ve all realized it at this point,” the man in the black hood, still grinning and looking like Mr. Mitsuo, replied patiently. “Since you’re smart. Ha-ha-ha, hm~.”

He cracked his neck with a pop. As Shuu stepped in front to protect us, it looked like Kanata was pondering things. Was there anything I could do?

“In any case, I’m shocked. I never thought you all would appear in front of me, equipped with knowledge about Anazumu.”

“Well, we’re the ones who should be shocked. To think there was an evil god hidden in our neighborhood.”

I mean, who would ever assume that such a weapon of mass destruction was sealed close to their house? Sure, there were strange stories about it, but anyone would’ve assumed that it was just an ordinary Jizou statue. And this was the result.

“Leaving aside the future, fate is out of the gods’ hands, too. That so many coincidences aligned surprises even me. No matter how you look at it, for that guy to… No, never mind. You’ve already gathered a great deal of information, so you won’t need my explanation, will you?”

I was wondering who he was talking about, but he told us that we didn’t need any further explanations. I couldn’t help thinking that our life was quite unusual.

The evil god held the vajra tightly and put his other hand on his chest. Then he stopped grinning. Even though he still looked like a clown, his atmosphere changed to a solemn one.

“So, I will skip the explanation about how evil gods work. I am Shiva, the God of Destruction. Since there is already a god on Earth with this name, you might also call me Asura, if you want[1](#easy-footnote-bottom-1-121112).”

Shiva, the God of Destruction. The last of the three evil gods. Somehow, he seemed more like you could talk things out with him compared to the other evil gods so far. He didn’t display any hostility to begin with.

“You might want to introduce yourselves, but I already know all of you other than this wolfkin girl. In any case, that was quite the close call.”

“What do you…?”

“Oh, I’m talking about back when she came to pray to this statue together with Shuu.”

Rir pointed at herself while tilting her head in confusion. By “back then”, he probably meant the time she had tried to pray to the statue and started to act strangely.

“I sensed Anazumu’s magic power, so I thought of taking her over as a temporary host until the Guide arrived, but… Shuu was close and called out to her frantically, so I stopped.”

“U-Uhm…”

“Incidentally, if I had taken her over like this, she’d only have lived for another three days, and it further would have destroyed her mind.”

“Th-Thank you…?”

What was going on? He really seemed quite reasonable compared to the evil gods we had met so far. Rather, he’d been treating us awfully friendly.

“If I were to possess someone other than the Guide or people from the bloodline who designate them, they would quickly fall apart. Though the Hero, Sage, and the bloodlines connected to them would work, too… That reminds me, five of you were sent to Anazumu. I assume at least one of you is a Sage, right? Who is it? Don’t be shy and raise your hand.”

Shuu, Kanata, and Sakura looked at each other. As a result of that short exchange, they apparently decided to tell him without making a fuss. All three of them raised their hands slightly.

“Oh!? Shuu, Kanata, and Sakura are Sages? Should I call this an abundant harvest?”

He seemed genuinely surprised, without any lies or pretenses. It sounded like, even for an evil god, the emergence of three Sages at once was a rare occasion.

“Somehow, this whole situation feels wrong,” Kanata spoke up. “I’d like to ask something.”

He had been pondering for a while, so it would be best to let him speak.

“…Uhm, you know about us, don’t you, Shiva?”

“Hm? Yes, I know a lot about you! I’ve known Ayumu and Mika since they were little. I remember them bringing Shuu along when they enrolled in pre-school. As for you, Kanata and Sakura, I learned about you when you were just a few weeks old.”

“How can you know that much about us?”

The evil god’s reply to that question was simple.

“Why, I’ve seen you.”

#### **Footnotes:**

1. [Asuras](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Asura) are evil/destructive demigod-like beings in Hinduism, which feels a good parallel to Anazumu’s evil gods compared to proper gods

+++

# **633 – Shiva, the God of Destruction – 1**

“You saw us… what do you mean by that?”

“Exactly what I said… To be honest, I couldn’t use the majority of my power while I was sealed in the vajra. But even with those restrictions, I could see what was happening outside.”

_Huh, I get it._

He was probably bored while sealed. It had been hundreds of years, after all. So, this was the reason he knew so much about us and that he treated us this kindly.

“It has been such a long time since I was sealed and I have seen all kinds of people, but your beauty, Ayumu, Mika, and Sakura, is unmatched. Then there is Kanata’s genius and Shuu, who’s so heroic, you might think he wasn’t an earthling but born in Anazumu instead.”

“Th-That makes sense.”

_Why did he include me along Mika and Sakura? He isn’t one of those who think I’m a girl, is he?_

“Anyway, what happened to the other two evil gods? All I know is that they both came back to life within a short span of time.”

What would be the best answer here? Could we be honest, considering the evil gods seemed to have some sense of camaraderie?

“…Heh-heh, as I thought, there is this scent. The scent of Surtr that’s coming from Shuu since some time. That disgusting, burnt scent… You are a Sage, aren’t you, Shuu? Could it be that you were possessed once?”

“Well, yes. You could say that he took me over…”

“What!?”

That sounded like genuine shock. He looked he was about to ask “Seriously?”

“D-Does that mean, the berserker is currently inside you, Shuu?”

“Well… about that.”

Shuu gave Kanata a glance. My brother stepped forward to explain.

“He has already been defeated and then sealed.”

“What, seriously? You’re not lying?”

“D-Dead serious…”

I had been putting myself mentally on guard, assuming a fight was imminent, but this whole situation was off. Up to this point, the evil gods had either acted like arrogant deities or battle-crazed monsters, so one of them talking rationally and mixing in modern expressions felt anticlimactic.

“How did you manage to take that guy down? He’s the strongest of us three.”

“That’s Bro and Mika-nee for you.”

“Huh, Ayumu and Mika… So, how did you do it?”

“Ah, well… several things happened…”

I was trying to play it down, but the moment I said it, it felt like the way Shiva looked at me changed. There seemed to be fear in his gaze.

“I do have another question regarding us evil gods. This guy I’m possessing is the Guide who returned to Earth, but it feels like his body was previously used by Samaeyl. How did that come to pass?”

“Are you unable to access the memories of those you possess?” Kanata asked without any hesitation. “I mean, he manages a circus, how could you do that without them?”

“I can, but I usually give him back control over his mind and body,” Shiva replied with just as little hesitation.

“So, when we called you…?”

“That was me imitating him. Was I convincing?”

_W-Was he convincing, he asks.._.

“Yes… quite. But how did you know the things only Mr. Mitsuo and I should know?”

“Just as I mentioned earlier; I looked at just his recent memories for when you interacted.”

“In that case, take some time and read the memories of Mr. Mitsuo’s time in Anazumu. Then you’ll know what happened to Samaeyl.”

“I see. Would you give me a moment, everyone?”

Shiva closed his eyes and likely started to trace his host’s memories. Mr. Mitsuo was probably the one who knew most about Samaeyl. About five minutes later, he opened his eyes again.

Incidentally, we talked strategy, meanwhile.

“Hrm… so that was what happened. I understand it for the most part. Incredible… Indeed, you’re the Levelmaker, Ayumu…”

“What is this Levelmaker?”

I was genuinely curious. I had no idea what this word was meant to signify… With the word “level” in the name, it felt a bit like a compliment for someone obsessed by leveling up like me.

“Uhm… well, about that. It’s something like a respectful title for someone who got strong by leveling up like crazy. Definitely.”

“I see!”

_So, it is a compliment, after all. Heh-heh._

It felt like he held some things back, but for now this was enough for me.

“Well, there are more important things.”

The evil god’s body suddenly started to tremble and gave off a frightening aura. Was he dissatisfied with something?

_Right, I’m the one who defeated his two friends, so…_

“Ayumu, you’re not a girl!?”

“Huh…!”

“Didn’t you tell this Guide called Mitsuo that you’re male? What the hell is going on!?”

_Oh, he’s actually one of those who thought I’m a girl? But you know?_

“Uhm… I’m pretty sure I always wore a boy’s school uniform when I came to visit here, ever since I enrolled in middle school…”

“I thought you were cross-dressing! And here I was getting all excited…! Who’d have thought you’re a femboy. Oh, well, it’s fine.”

_What the hell is it with this guy? I can’t tell anymore._

+++

# **634 – Shiva, the God of Destruction – 2**

“Hm…? Hang on.”

“What’s wrong?”

After learning that I was a femboy, Shiva inclined his head as if he was wondering about something.

“If you’re not a girl, Ayumu, that means the relationship between you is quite a bit different, isn’t it? I saw Kanata and Sakura on a date in the zoo, after all… She never went there before since she was blind, right?”

“Right, about that…”

Kanata briefly explained how Sakura’s eyesight had been restored, without going into much detail. When he did that, Shiva started to tear up.

“I see… I get it, it happened in Anazumu… You were lucky in several ways… Thinking of how you looked after and protected Sakura when she couldn’t see, I just can’t hold back my tears…”

“Uhm… yes… thank you… for caring?”

Sakura’s words of thanks appeared more like a question. It was understandable, we were dealing with an evil god, after all. The previous two had been our enemies.

“Gotcha… I can’t wait to see your kids. They’ll be sure to be world-class beauties… or handsome guys.”

“W-Well, you’ll still have to wait six or more years for that…”

“That’s true. Even a god like me wouldn’t give my blessing to a pregnancy at 14. Well, the two of you would be fine either way, and I’m not one who can bestow blessings in the first place.”

_Where the hell is he going with this? He’s actually talking like some grandpa from the neighborhood. This feels wrong, completely off._

It even threw Kanata off.

“Anyway, the main thing I wanted ask about is whether Ayumu and Mika are dating… Come to think of it, they did kiss.”

“And when you saw that, you assumed…”

“Mika was a lesbian trying to win Ayumu over.”

“I see.”

Still, we had never kissed in front of the Jizou statue. Well, given the way he talked earlier, it was probably safe to assume that he could observe whatever place he wanted.

“Alright… I thought for sure that Ayumu would end up with Shuu and Mika would give up since they’re the same gender. Makes sense, Mika never was interested in girls.”

“You… you’re off! That’s not how things went!”

If I was a genuine girl, then that really would make Mika a lesbian. Well… he wasn’t completely wrong since we had kissed in Anazumu while I was female.

_Not like I can say that out loud now. Absolutely not._

“That means, Shuu’s sweetheart is this wolfkin…”

“R-Rir…”

“Right, Rir.”

Shiva tried to smile as if to put her at ease, but it failed since he was still in clown make-up.

“By the way, Shuu. Surtr can only take over either a Sage filled with true fury or someone of the lineage who can summon Sages… How in the world did they manage to enrage you? Did something happen to Ayumu and Mika when you were over there? Based on experience, the majority of the lineage able to summon Sages have nasty personalities.”

“Oh… no, it was Surtr himself who did something to Rir…”

“So, he turned her to ash? How tragic… In that case, how is she alive right now? I could ask Ayumu and Mika the same. How are you alive after coming in contact with Samaeyl’s feathers? How is this possible? Both cause instant death and should be irreversible by either revival medicine or magic.”

Instant death attacks with no possibility of resurrection. It was easy to guess why he considered those genuinely devastating… if you didn’t have access to Amritas. To begin with, we owed those potions a great deal for being able to spend our lives so comfortably.

“Yes, we used Amritas on the corpses. Well, Ayumu did mostly.”

“Yup.”

“I see, so you managed to discover such valuable medicine… Still, it’s strange. Normally, no one would have more than ten bottles of those at hand, but this host remembers you bringing the full populace of a country back to life.”

“I managed that because I can mass produce them.”

“You mass produce them!? What in the world!?”

He seemed incredibly shocked. Even more than when he learned I was male.

“Mass producing Amritas… Do you understand what you’re doing!?”

“Uhm, I usually only share them with friends and family. Is that an issue?”

That wasn’t completely correct. Since I also made them available to the king and his friends.

“Well… it is **the** divine restoration item, able to grant eternal youth and rejuvenation, able to bring even those back to life in perfect condition who originally should never have been able to come back.”

“I mean, that’s why I don’t just hand them out and manage them pretty carefully.”

I kept the fact to myself that I pretty much guzzled them down like soft drinks until the king pointed this out. I’d probably get scolded otherwise.

“I guess this works. In any case, I was worried that anything happened to you…”

“Wh-Why do you care so much about us?”

“I mean, it’s because I’ve known you since you were little.”

_So, he’s genuinely like some old man from the neighborhood? This is all wrong… geez._

“By the way…”

“Hrm, what is it, Kanata?”

“This might be blunt, but are you ultimately our enemy, Shiva? Or are you a friend?” Kanata boldly asked. “The other two evil gods were hostile to us.”

I checked the time. Had it really just been 30 minutes since we left the house?

“Well, about that.”

+++

# **635 – Like a Friendly Old Man from the Neighborhood**

“How could I ever hurt the kids I’ve known since they were little?” the evil god bluntly replied.

It seemed genuine.

“Don’t lump me together with those two guys in the first place. Samaeyl might lead the demons, but she’d kill any human without a second thought unless it was someone she’d acknowledged. And Surtr is a battle-crazed maniac. Without any mercy or such.”

“…I understand, so Samaeyl is the leader type and Surtr the fighter type. What about you?”

“I’m a free spirit.”

Indeed, this seemed to fit him to a tee. Like how he frequently changed the subject mid-conversation to what interested him.

“But you must’ve done something bad for them to seal you away on Earth.”

“Yes, back in the past, I didn’t care about anyone but a select few, just like Samaeyl. I did just as many bad things as them, stuff worthy of an evil god. Though I’m still the one who killed the least people, you see?”

Well, with her special skill, Samaeyl probably had the highest body count.

“Why are you so open with all that?”

“I’ve been here since the start of the Edo period[1](#easy-footnote-bottom-1-121251). Since then, all~ I’ve done is observe Japan. There were many wars… but it has been peaceful for several decades now. Being in the midst of this peace… it caused my disposition to turn peaceful, too.”

Come to think of it, this man (?) had watched Japan for more than 400 years. An unimaginably vast difference of time separated us. Well, if we became immortal by drinking Amritas in Anazumu, then we could experience this, too.

“Seriously?”

“Cross my heart. Well, to begin with you’ve crushed Samaeyl and Surtr… mainly Ayumu, I guess. It doesn’t feel like I stand a chance against you. At all.”

He wasn’t wrong. If both of them were to attack us at the same time now, I was confident we’d manage.

“Can’t evil gods use magic on this side? That way, you could take us out while we’re weak.”

“Hm~, that’s another thing… Even if it was a situation where I’d be forced to do that, I wouldn’t want to. Using our abilities here is incredibly difficult, so even if I tried to conquer the world with this limited power… the military strength of a single country on earth would be overwhelmingly higher.”

_Huh, so evil gods do have limitations, after all? Though the fact that he compares things on a national level is kinda scary._

“You’re not lying?”

“I’m not. Kanata, please believe me on this as an old acquaintance, even if I can’t prove it.”

That might have been a cool line, but it didn’t work with that clown make-up… it just looked silly. Anyway, I could probably leave things to Kanata here.

“I can’t honestly say that I trust you, but… you’ve been acting clearly differently from other evil gods so far. Let’s head home for today, Shiva. Is everyone alright with that?”

I nodded.

Sakura did the same. Mika looked at what I did and then nodded too, while Shuu looked at Kanata silently without giving any reply. Rir kept staring at Shiva with wide eyes.

“It looks like this works… That said, what will happen to Mr. Mitsuo if you keep possessing him? He has his own life…”

“Oh, that’s true. I snuck out without telling the other troupe members.”

“What do we do? Can you go back into the varja?”

“By myself? If I go in there willingly, I can take over anyone I’ve previously possessed anytime I want. Are you sure we should do that?”

“It works for today. Could you return to the circus and go back into the vajra temporarily?”

“…Alright.” Shiva turned around. “The time will likely come when all of you properly seal me, but when that happens… could you modify the vajra so I can watch what happens outside and talk to people? Anyway, I’ll be off.”

With those words, he dissolved into darkness. Well, he was simply walking away, but his jacket made it look that way.

“…Didn’t expect things to turn out like this,” Shuu muttered.

“Even I genuinely didn’t anticipate this,” Kanata replied. “At worst, I thought of us talking our way out of it if he turned out aggressive. There was no reason for that.”

“B-But is that truly fine? What do you think, Big Sis?”

“Me? Well, probably? He doesn’t feel like an enemy.”

Was this what Mika’s intuition, which accurately predicted that we’d met the man in the black hood this week, told her? Then it was likely fine.

“Have we really been standin’ for a full 40 minutes in this chill?”

“Are you cold, Shuu? Do you want me to hug you? Though my body temperature isn’t high either…”

“Nah, I ain’t cold, let’s just hold hands. It’s a bit hard to walk while huggin’… Anyway, we’ll be headin’ home.”

They took each other’s hands. Rir looked quite happy.

“Alright, good night to you, then.”

“Woof, good night.”

“Good night, you guys.”

The two of them left.

The remaining four of us decided to make our ways to our respective homes, too. It somehow felt like we’d gotten rid of a burden. Tomorrow, we’d go normally to school again.

Still, dealing with evil gods was always a hassle and it would likely only get worse from now on, though that couldn’t be helped. At least he wasn’t overtly hostile, which made it a million times better.

#### **Footnotes:**

1. Around 1600 AD in the western calendar

++++

## **Boundary Labyrinth and the Foreign Magician - 184 – A New Life**

We were training with our companions in a corner of the courtyard as the morning sun streamed in.

The courtyard had become quite spacious, making it easy to summon Lindwurm whenever we wanted. I wondered if having Lindwurm observe our training regularly might help improve our coordination.

Lindwurm was letting the Carbuncles ride on its nose and tail, sliding them around playfully. It seemed to be leisurely sunbathing… but in reality, it was watching our training with keen interest. That shouldn’t be a problem.

Incidentally, Fortok told me that the Carbuncles avoid riding on Lindwurm’s back because Lindwurm dislikes having anyone other than me on its back. How dutiful.

“It’s swelling. Dangerous.”

Sheila issued a brief warning. As if responding to her words, the Aqua Golem appeared to swell from within before bursting, scattering water droplets everywhere.

Our companions blocked them with the Shield Magic Tools equipped on their left hands. In actual combat, there’s no guarantee that someone’s warning will reach in time. Faster than thought. They need to be able to deploy them instantly.

What we’re doing is preparing for our visit to the Blazing Fortress. We’ve incorporated combat scenarios anticipating battles at the Blazing Fortress into our morning training sessions.

“That one was a bit dangerous.”

“Perhaps Lavigne and I should create more cover.”

Grace and Ashley were discussing while Marlene seemed to be reflecting on her Saucer’s movements—nodding as she performed mental training, moving her rapier like a conductor’s baton in small motions. Well, since everyone defended themselves, there was no damage this time.

“Um. Maybe Sheila and I should move together so we can hear her warnings from the direction we need to be alert?”

“Shall we try that next time?”

“…I see. Countermeasures for Bomb Rocks.”

Claudia, who had been watching the training, nodded with admiration. Yes. There are rock monsters that perform suicide attacks. While the Fire Rat coat protects against heat damage, we still need to deal with the rock fragments.

“Well, we should make sure to conduct thorough rehearsals.”

While my companions continue their training, I must carry out my own in parallel.

I covered my eyes with cloth and positioned Golems around me. They were set to automatic pilot, performing coordinated attacks according to pre-set algorithms.

I didn’t link my vision with Caduceus. By watching my companions’ training through Caduceus, I could operate and supervise the Golems while conducting my own training simultaneously.

Meanwhile, my training involved sensing attacks through thin Shields deployed around my body and continuously dodging them by a hair’s breadth.

From the angle and force of attacks hitting my Shields, I could determine the Golems’ stances. I targeted only their heads, shattering them with Ouroboros. An attack from a Golem behind me. I twisted my body to evade while touching its head and simultaneously delivering a shock Strike.

The Golems countered with feints like Water Bullets meant to appear as Strikes, water whips formed from transformed hands attacking from outside my range, self-destruct explosions, and time-delayed attacks using overlapping bodies.

I continued intercepting and dodging while dismantling and shattering the Aqua Golems.

Smooth activation of shock Strikes, detecting attacks from blind spots with omnidirectional Shields. Having reached a satisfactory level with these aspects, I landed on the ground and removed my blindfold.

“I had heard rumors that you were the Demon Slayer, master… I’m not sure whether to be convinced or astonished.”

Cecilia was wide-eyed. The Labyrinth Village residents studying work with her were the same. The children were watching with sparkling eyes. Hmm… It’s slightly embarrassing.

“All I can do is admire. You should have much to learn. Make sure to observe carefully during your work breaks.”

“Yes, Mihaela-sama.”

The two had mentioned something about having self-defense knowledge.

In that case, I should probably familiarize myself with their Weapons and fighting styles. Well, while Mihaela is obvious, Cecilia also has work within the household, so I’m not planning to take her into the Labyrinth.

“Mihaela-san uses a rapier, right?”

“Only as a hobby.”

She’s being modest, but her posture—or rather, her core stability—doesn’t waver. I get the feeling she might actually be quite skilled.

“Then, Cecilia too?”

“No. I practiced with the Weapon my father used because I wanted to be able to use it myself.”

With that, Cecilia brought out the Weapon she uses to show me.

…If the handle were a bit longer, it would probably be classified as a pole weapon like a glaive or bardiche. The handle is somewhat short, seemingly designed for closer combat.

“This is for indoor use. In more open spaces, I replace it with a longer handle. Even without much physical strength, you can generate power with momentum.”

“I see.”

“I’ve taught her body maneuvering and unarmed self-defense techniques—things with practical applications. As a servant, she should be considered adequate.”

Well… she doesn’t look like she’d lose to your average thief. The fact that she wasn’t taught rapier skills was probably out of respect for her own wishes.

“Still, perhaps we should assume that flying will be a prerequisite from now on. I’m already too old for that kind of fighting style.”

Mihaela said with her eyes closed.

Hmm. Maybe I should prepare Aerial Combat Gear for both of them too. What Mihaela means is fighting while flying around, but even just being able to adjust altitude against opponents using Shields as footholds would make a difference.

“When you have free time from work, would you two like to join us for training?”

“Wouldn’t we be intruding?”

“If I increase the number of Golems, it just becomes more Magic training, so it’s no problem.”

“In other words… you still have room to spare in your Magic control.”

Claudia smiled.

“Hello—”

“Hello, Theo-kun.”

“Wow, this has become quite the mansion.”

At dusk, Justia and Dominique came to visit with Forestbird’s Escort.

Or rather, they came to practice music with Irmhild.

The stage is already taking shape, and while everyone enjoys the performance, we thought it would be good for them to develop interest in the theater too, so they decided to do light practice in the recreation room.

While they played music, everyone relaxed in the recreation room. Perhaps matching the atmosphere, Irmhild and the others were playing lively, cheerful music.

“You’ve made all sorts of things, haven’t you?”

“Yeah, well. Since we have the opportunity, I’d be happy if you’d stay and enjoy yourselves.”

Forestbird are good-natured folks, so they might be just the right people for the Labyrinth Village residents to interact with outsiders.

“Huh? Throwing darts at a target to reduce points? Sounds fun. Fitz, let’s have a match.”

“Sure. What shall we wager?”

“Drinks on the loser when we get back.”

“You’re on.”

Since we made several dartboards, they could play on an available one. The two who immediately showed interest in darts seemed to be enjoying themselves playing alongside the Labyrinth Village residents.

“Is that girl using the Humanization Spell like Justia-san and Dominique-san?”

Lucian said while looking at the Arachne girl named Claire, who was smiling happily while playing cards with companions at a table. She’s one of the monsters who can’t use the Humanization Spell and relies on Magic Tools instead.

She has several black pearl-like shines on her forehead… but apparently those aren’t Ornaments—they’re spider eyes. They look like a Circlet and don’t feel particularly intimidating in appearance. She herself gives off a quiet impression too.

“Yeah. Well, almost all the servants do. In her case, she relies on Magic Tools.”

“Is that so?”

Lucian murmured with admiration.

Incidentally, Monica also joined the darts match and ended up overwhelming both Robin and Fitz. It seems Monica, being in charge of scouting, has the best throwing skills in Forestbird.

Robin and Fitz, who were resigned to having to treat everyone, received wry smiles from the Labyrinth Village residents, creating quite a peaceful scene.

While enjoying Irmhild’s performance and watching this scene, Alfred contacted me through the Communication Device.

『I tried reaching out through connections. They said they definitely want to hear Theo-kun’s story.』

『Understood. How about I show them some of the things I’ve made?』

『Roger. Where should we meet?』

There was an immediate response from the other side after I replied. Alfred seems to be getting quite familiar with operating the Communication Device.

『I think the workshop and my house are still too early for that, so I’ll bring things over.』

『Understood. I’ll contact you again once the schedule is set.』
